        aria-controls="page-body"
        tabindex="${selected ? "0" : "-1"}"
        data-tab-group="${escapeHTML(group)}"
        data-tab-id="${escapeHTML(id)}"
        data-tab-index="${escapeHTML(index)}"
        data-tab-count="${escapeHTML(total)}"
        ${legacyAttr}
      >${escapeHTML(label)}</button>
    `;
  }

  function requestConfirmation(options) {
    const next = {
      ...defaultConfirmDialog(),
      ...options,
      open: true,
    };
    state.confirmDialog = next;
    renderConfirmDialog();
  }

  function closeConfirmationDialog() {
    const dialog = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog");
    if (dialog && dialog.open) {
      dialog.close("cancel");
    }
    const selector = state.confirmDialog.returnFocusSelector;
    const focusID = state.confirmDialog.returnFocusID;
    state.confirmDialog = defaultConfirmDialog();
    if (selector) {
      document.querySelector(selector)?.focus();
    } else if (focusID) {
      document.querySelector(`[data-focus-id="${focusID}"]`)?.focus();
    }
  }

  function renderConfirmDialog() {
    const dialog = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog");
    if (!dialog) return;
    const title = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-title");
    const message = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-message");
    const confirm = document.getElementById("confirm-dialog-confirm");
    if (!title || !message || !confirm) return;
    title.textContent = defaultString(state.confirmDialog.title, "Confirm Action");
    message.textContent = defaultString(state.confirmDialog.message, "Review this action before continuing.");
    confirm.textContent = defaultString(state.confirmDialog.confirmLabel, "Confirm");
    confirm.className = state.confirmDialog.tone === "danger" ? "tx-btn tx-btn-danger" : "tx-btn tx-btn-primary";
    if (state.confirmDialog.open && !dialog.open) {
      dialog.showModal();
      confirm.focus();
      return;
    }
    if (!state.confirmDialog.open && dialog.open) {
      dialog.close("cancel");
    }
  }

  function renderStatePill(attentionState, status) {
    return `<span class="run-state-pill run-state-${escapeHTML(defaultString(attentionState, "active"))}">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status, "-"))}</span>`;
  }

  function pauseStateSummary(pauseUntil, pauseReason) {
    const until = String(pauseUntil || "").trim();
    const reason = String(pauseReason || "").trim();
    const parts = [];
    if (until) {
      const formatted = formatDateTime(until);
      parts.push(formatted || until);
    }
    if (reason) {
      parts.push(reason);
    }
    return parts.join(" · ");
  }

  function renderStatePillWithPause(attentionState, status, pauseUntil, pauseReason) {
    const detail = pauseStateSummary(pauseUntil, pauseReason);
    if (!detail) {
      return renderStatePill(attentionState, status);
    }
    return `${renderStatePill(attentionState, status)}<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(detail)}</span>`;
  }

  function runRepoDisplay(run) {
    if (run && String(run.repo_slug || "").trim()) {
      return String(run.repo_slug).trim();
    }
    return defaultString(run && run.repo_label, defaultString(run && run.repo_name, "Standalone"));
  }

  function dropRepo(repoSlug) {
    const slug = String(repoSlug || "").trim();
    if (!slug) return;
    requestConfirmation({
      title: `Drop ${slug}?`,
      message: "This removes tracked repo state, queued work, and managed sandboxes from the workspace.",
      confirmLabel: "Drop Repo",
      tone: "danger",
      onConfirm() {
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${slug}/drop`, {
          method: "POST",
        }).then(() => {
          if (state.logDrawer) {
            state.logDrawer.close();
          }
          if (state.workItemDrawer) {
            state.workItemDrawer.close();
          }
          Promise.allSettled([load(), loadAttention({ silent: true })]);
          toast("success", "Repo dropped", slug);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Repo drop failed", error.message);
        });
      },
    });
  }

  function renderSurface(title, copy, bodyHTML, options = {}) {
    const extraClass = options.className ? ` ${options.className}` : "";
    return `
      <section class="surface${extraClass}">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>${escapeHTML(title)}</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(copy)}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${bodyHTML}
      </section>
    `;
  }

  function renderSurfacePair(sections) {
    const items = sections.filter(Boolean);
    if (!items.length) return "";
    if (items.length === 1) return items[0];
    return `<section class="layout-two-col">${items.join("")}</section>`;
  }

  function renderSidebar() {
    const nav = document.getElementById("sidebar-nav");
    const repos = sortedRepos();
    const homeActive = state.currentView === "home";
    const homeCount = state.attention.loaded
      ? (state.attention.items || []).length
      : pendingRuns().length + pendingWorkItems().length;
    const repoQuery = String(state.sidebarQuery || "").trim().toLowerCase();
    const visibleRepos = repos.filter((repo) => !repoQuery || repo.repo_slug.toLowerCase().includes(repoQuery));
    nav.innerHTML = `
      <div class="sidebar-nav-shell">
        <label class="selector sidebar-search">
          <span>Find Repo</span>
          <input type="search" value="${escapeHTML(state.sidebarQuery)}" placeholder="owner/repo" data-sidebar-query="true" />
        </label>
        <div class="nav-main-links" role="navigation" aria-label="Workspace views">
          <button class="nav-item ${homeActive ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="home" aria-current="${homeActive ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Attention</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${homeCount}</span>
          </button>
          <button class="nav-item ${state.currentView === "usage" ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="usage" aria-current="${state.currentView === "usage" ? "page" : "false"}">
            <span class="nav-label">Usage</span>
            <span class="nav-count">${usageNavCount()}</span>
          </button>
        </div>
        <details class="nav-disclosure" ${state.currentView === "repo" || repoQuery ? "open" : ""}>
          <summary>Repos</summary>
          <div class="nav-disclosure-body">
            <button class="nav-item" type="button" data-open-onboard="true">
              <span class="nav-label">Onboard Repo</span>
              <span class="nav-count">+</span>
            </button>
            ${visibleRepos.length ? visibleRepos.map((repo) => {
              const active = state.currentView === "repo" && state.selectedRepo === repo.repo_slug;
              return `
                <button class="nav-item ${active ? "nav-item-active" : ""}" type="button" data-nav-view="repo" data-repo-slug="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}" aria-current="${active ? "page" : "false"}">
                  <span class="nav-label">${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}</span>
                  <span class="nav-count">${outstandingRepoCount(repo)}</span>
                </button>
              `;
            }).join("") : `<p class="empty-copy">${repoQuery ? "No repos match this filter." : "No repos are onboarded yet."}</p>`}
          </div>
        </details>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderHeader() {
    const title = document.getElementById("page-title");
    const subtitle = document.getElementById("page-subtitle");
    const updated = document.getElementById("overview-updated");

    if (!state.overview) {
      if (state.currentView === "usage") {
        title.textContent = "Usage";
        if (state.overviewError) {
          subtitle.textContent = "Usage data can still load while the workspace overview is unavailable.";
          updated.textContent = "Overview unavailable.";
        } else if (state.usage.error) {
          subtitle.textContent = "Usage data failed while the workspace overview is still loading.";
          updated.textContent = "Overview still loading.";
        } else if (state.usage.loaded) {
          subtitle.textContent = "Usage data is ready while the workspace overview is still loading.";
          updated.textContent = "Overview still loading.";
        } else {
          subtitle.textContent = "Loading usage data and workspace overview.";
          updated.textContent = "Waiting for state...";
        }
      } else {
        title.textContent = "Attention";
        subtitle.textContent = state.overviewError ? "Attention inbox is unavailable." : "Loading the operator inbox...";
        updated.textContent = state.overviewError ? "Overview unavailable." : "Waiting for state...";
      }
      return;
    }

    updated.textContent = `Updated ${formatDateTime(state.overview.generated_at)}`;

    if (state.currentView === "home") {
      title.textContent = "Attention";
      subtitle.textContent = "Single inbox for approvals, findings, blocked work, and operator decisions.";
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      title.textContent = "Usage";
      subtitle.textContent = "Token spend across NANA-managed sessions, lanes, phases, and activity buckets.";
      return;
    }

    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    if (!repo) {
      title.textContent = "Attention";
      subtitle.textContent = "Single inbox for approvals, findings, blocked work, and operator decisions.";
      return;
    }

    title.textContent = repo.repo_slug;
    subtitle.textContent = state.repoTab === "controls"
      ? "Repo-scoped scheduling, findings inbox management, and markdown import review."
      : state.repoTab === "scouts"
        ? "Scout-discovered items, proposal details, and repo-local management actions."
      : state.repoTab === "config"
        ? "Start-facing repo configuration and participation controls."
        : "Repo queue posture, pending jobs, and tracked work.";
  }

  function renderTabs() {
    const host = document.getElementById("page-tabs");
    if (state.currentView !== "repo" || !selectedRepoSummary()) {
      host.removeAttribute("role");
      host.removeAttribute("aria-label");
      host.innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }
    host.setAttribute("role", "tablist");
    host.setAttribute("aria-label", "Repo sections");
    host.innerHTML = [
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "overview", "Overview", state.repoTab === "overview", 0, 4),
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "scouts", "Scouts", state.repoTab === "scouts", 1, 4),
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "config", "Config", state.repoTab === "config", 2, 4),
      tabButtonMarkup("repo", "controls", "Controls", state.repoTab === "controls", 3, 4),
    ].join("");
  }

  function repoOverviewRows() {
    return sortedRepos().map((repo) => ({
      repo_slug: repo.repo_slug,
      mode: `${defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "unknown")} / ${defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "unknown")}`,
      queued_issues: repo.issue_counts.queued || 0,
      blocked_issues: repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0,
      service_queue: (repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) + (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0),
      scout_queue: repoScoutQueueCount(repo),
      planned_queue: repoManualPlannedQueueCount(repo),
      pending_runs: pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug).length,
    }));
  }

  function runGridRows(runs, includeRepo) {
    return runs.map((run) => {
      const row = {
        run_id: run.run_id,
        backend: defaultString(run.backend, "-"),
        work_type: workTypeLabel(run.work_type),
        status: defaultString(run.status, "active"),
        attention_state: defaultString(run.attention_state, "active"),
        pause_reason: defaultString(run.pause_reason, ""),
        pause_until: defaultString(run.pause_until, ""),
        current_phase: defaultString(run.current_phase, "Awaiting phase"),
        current_round: run.current_round || 0,
        updated_at: formatDateTime(run.updated_at),
      };
      if (row.pause_until) {
        row.current_phase = `Retry ${formatDateTime(row.pause_until)}`;
      } else if (row.current_round > 0) {
        row.current_phase = `${row.current_phase} · Round ${row.current_round}`;
      }
      if (includeRepo) {
        row.repo_slug = runRepoDisplay(run);
      }
      return row;
    });
  }

  function workItemRows(items, includeRepo) {
    return items.map((item) => {
      const row = {
        id: item.id,
        source: `${defaultString(item.source, "-")}/${defaultString(item.source_kind, "-")}`,
        status: defaultString(item.status, "-"),
        attention_state: defaultString(item.attention_state, "active"),
        pause_reason: defaultString(item.pause_reason, ""),
        pause_until: defaultString(item.pause_until, ""),
        subject: defaultString(item.subject, "(no subject)"),
        updated_at: formatDateTime(item.updated_at),
        draft_kind: defaultString(item.draft_kind, "-"),
      };
      if (includeRepo) {
        row.repo_slug = defaultString(item.repo_slug, "Standalone");
      }
      return row;
    });
  }

  function pendingRunColumns(includeRepo) {
    const columns = [];
    if (includeRepo) {
      columns.push({ field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo" });
    }
    columns.push(
      { field: "backend", label: "Backend" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "current_phase", label: "Phase" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      { field: "run_id", label: "Logs", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-log-run-id="{{run_id}}">Logs</button>' },
    );
    return columns;
  }

  function workRunRows(runs, includeRepo) {
    return runs.map((run) => {
      const row = {
        run_id: run.run_id,
        backend: defaultString(run.backend, "-"),
        kind: defaultString(run.backend, "-"),
        status: defaultString(run.status, "active"),
        attention_state: defaultString(run.attention_state, "active"),
        pause_reason: defaultString(run.pause_reason, ""),
        pause_until: defaultString(run.pause_until, ""),
        current_phase: defaultString(run.current_phase, "Awaiting phase"),
        current_round: run.current_round || 0,
        target_url: defaultString(run.target_url, "-"),
        updated_at: formatDateTime(run.updated_at),
        can_sync: run.backend === "github",
        can_resolve: Boolean(run.resolve_allowed),
      };
      if (row.pause_until) {
        row.current_phase = `Retry ${formatDateTime(row.pause_until)}`;
      } else if (row.current_round > 0) {
        row.current_phase = `${row.current_phase} · Round ${row.current_round}`;
      }
      if (includeRepo) {
        row.repo_slug = runRepoDisplay(run);
      }
      return row;
    });
  }

  function workRunColumns(includeRepo) {
    const columns = [];
    if (includeRepo) {
      columns.push({ field: "repo_slug", label: "Repo" });
    }
    columns.push(
      { field: "backend", label: "Backend" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "current_phase", label: "Phase" },
      { field: "target_url", label: "Target" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      { field: "run_id", label: "Open", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-log-run-id="{{run_id}}">Open</button>' },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Sync",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (!row.can_sync) {
            return '<span class="data-value-text">N/A</span>';
          }
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Sync</button>`;
        },
      },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Resolve",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          if (!row.can_resolve) {
            return '<span class="data-value-text">N/A</span>';
          }
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-resolve="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Resolve</button>`;
        },
      },
      {
        field: "run_id",
        label: "Drop",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          return `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-run-drop="${escapeHTML(row.run_id)}">Drop</button>`;
        },
      },
    );
    return columns;
  }

  function interpolateTemplate(template, row) {
    return String(template || "").replace(/\{\{\s*([^}\s]+)\s*\}\}/g, (_, key) => {
      const value = row && Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(row, key) ? row[key] : "";
      return escapeHTML(value);
    });
  }

  function rowSelectionMeta(row, options) {
    if (typeof options.rowSelect !== "function") {
      return null;
    }
    return options.rowSelect(row);
  }

  function renderGridCell(column, row, view) {
    if (typeof column.render === "function") {
      return column.render(row, view);
    }
    if (column.template) {
      return interpolateTemplate(column.template, row);
    }
    return `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(defaultString(row[column.field], "-"))}</span>`;
  }

  function renderGrid(target, columns, data, options = {}) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    const nextRenderKey = defaultString(options.renderKey, "");
    if (nextRenderKey && host.getAttribute("data-grid-render-key") === nextRenderKey) {
      return;
    }
    const currentTableWrap = options.preserveScroll ? host.querySelector(".data-table-wrap") : null;
    const currentCards = options.preserveScroll ? host.querySelector(".data-cards") : null;
    const tableScrollTop = currentTableWrap ? currentTableWrap.scrollTop : 0;
    const tableScrollLeft = currentTableWrap ? currentTableWrap.scrollLeft : 0;
    const cardsScrollTop = currentCards ? currentCards.scrollTop : 0;
    host.innerHTML = "";
    if (!columns.length || !data.length) {
      host.innerHTML = buildInlineNotice(options.emptyMessage || "No data yet");
      if (nextRenderKey) {
        host.setAttribute("data-grid-render-key", nextRenderKey);
      } else {
        host.removeAttribute("data-grid-render-key");
      }
      return;
    }
    const tableRows = data.map((row) => {
      const selection = rowSelectionMeta(row, options);
      const attrs = selection
        ? ` class="data-row-selectable ${selection.selected ? "data-row-selected" : ""}" tabindex="0" role="button" data-row-select-kind="${escapeHTML(selection.kind)}" data-row-select-id="${escapeHTML(selection.value)}" aria-pressed="${selection.selected ? "true" : "false"}"`
        : "";
      return `
        <tr${attrs}>
          ${columns.map((column) => `<td>${renderGridCell(column, row, "table")}</td>`).join("")}
        </tr>
      `;
    }).join("");
    const cardRows = data.map((row) => {
      const selection = rowSelectionMeta(row, options);
      const detailRows = columns.filter((column) => !column.action).map((column) => {
        return `
          <div class="data-card-row">
            <span class="data-card-label">${escapeHTML(column.label)}</span>
            <div class="data-card-value">${renderGridCell(column, row, "card")}</div>
          </div>
        `;
      }).join("");
      const actionRows = columns.filter((column) => column.action).map((column) => renderGridCell(column, row, "card")).join("");
      return `
        <article class="data-card ${selection ? `data-card-selectable ${selection.selected ? "data-card-selected" : ""}` : ""}" ${selection ? `tabindex="0" role="button" data-row-select-kind="${escapeHTML(selection.kind)}" data-row-select-id="${escapeHTML(selection.value)}" aria-pressed="${selection.selected ? "true" : "false"}"` : ""}>
          ${detailRows}
          ${actionRows ? `<div class="data-card-actions">${actionRows}</div>` : ""}
        </article>
      `;
    }).join("");
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="data-panel">
        <div class="data-table-wrap" style="max-height: ${escapeHTML(options.maxHeight || "420px")};">
          <table class="data-table">
            <thead>
              <tr>${columns.map((column) => `<th>${escapeHTML(column.label)}</th>`).join("")}</tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>${tableRows}</tbody>
          </table>
        </div>
        <div class="data-cards">${cardRows}</div>
      </div>
    `;
    if (nextRenderKey) {
      host.setAttribute("data-grid-render-key", nextRenderKey);
    } else {
      host.removeAttribute("data-grid-render-key");
    }
    if (options.preserveScroll) {
      const nextTableWrap = host.querySelector(".data-table-wrap");
      const nextCards = host.querySelector(".data-cards");
      if (nextTableWrap) {
        nextTableWrap.scrollTop = tableScrollTop;
        nextTableWrap.scrollLeft = tableScrollLeft;
      }
      if (nextCards) {
        nextCards.scrollTop = cardsScrollTop;
      }
    }
  }

  function renderPendingJobsChart(target, runs) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    const grouped = {};
    runs.forEach((run) => {
      const key = runRepoDisplay(run);
      grouped[key] = (grouped[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    const data = Object.entries(grouped)
      .map(([label, count]) => ({ label, count }))
      .sort((left, right) => right.count - left.count || left.label.localeCompare(right.label));
    if (!data.length) {
      destroyWidget(state.widgets[target]);
      delete state.widgets[target];
      delete state.widgetStateKeys[target];
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No pending jobs are active.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const chartOptions = {
      type: "bar",
      height: 300,
      title: "Pending jobs by repo",
      xAxis: { title: "Repo" },
      yAxis: { title: "Jobs" },
      series: [
        {
          name: "Pending jobs",
          data: data.map((item) => ({ x: item.label, y: item.count })),
        },
      ],
    };
    const nextKey = JSON.stringify(chartOptions.series);
    if (state.widgets[target] && state.widgetStateKeys[target] === nextKey) {
      return;
    }
    if (state.widgets[target] && typeof state.widgets[target].update === "function") {
      state.widgets[target].update(chartOptions);
      state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
      return;
    }
    replaceWidget(target, Teryx.chart(`#${target}`, chartOptions));
    state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
  }

  function renderUsageChart(target, chartOptions, emptyMessage) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    const hasData = Array.isArray(chartOptions.series) && chartOptions.series.some((series) => Array.isArray(series.data) && series.data.length);
    if (!hasData) {
      destroyWidget(state.widgets[target]);
      delete state.widgets[target];
      delete state.widgetStateKeys[target];
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(defaultString(emptyMessage, "No usage data is available."))}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    const nextKey = JSON.stringify(chartOptions.series);
    if (state.widgets[target] && state.widgetStateKeys[target] === nextKey) {
      return;
    }
    if (state.widgets[target] && typeof state.widgets[target].update === "function") {
      state.widgets[target].update(chartOptions);
      state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
      return;
    }
    replaceWidget(target, Teryx.chart(`#${target}`, chartOptions));
    state.widgetStateKeys[target] = nextKey;
  }

  function usageGroupChartData(groups, limit = 8) {
    return (groups || []).slice(0, limit).map((item) => ({
      x: item.key,
      y: Number(item.total_tokens || 0),
      label: item.key,
    }));
  }

  function usageDayChartData(groups) {
    return [ ...(groups || []) ]
      .sort((left, right) => String(left.key || "").localeCompare(String(right.key || "")))
      .map((item) => ({
        x: item.key,
        y: Number(item.total_tokens || 0),
        label: item.key,
      }));
  }

  function usageInsightsMarkup(insights) {
    if (!Array.isArray(insights) || !insights.length) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">No usage insights are available yet.</div>';
    }
    return `<ul class="usage-insights">${insights.map((insight) => `
      <li class="usage-insight">
        <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(insight.title, "Insight"))}</strong>
        <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(insight.summary, "(none)"))}</span>
        ${insight.command_hint ? `<code>${escapeHTML(insight.command_hint)}</code>` : ""}
      </li>
    `).join("")}</ul>`;
  }

  function syncUsageFilterControl(id, value) {
    const control = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!control || document.activeElement === control) return;
    const nextValue = String(value ?? "");
    if (control.value !== nextValue) {
      control.value = nextValue;
    }
  }

  function syncUsagePageState(filters) {
    const statusPill = document.getElementById("usage-status-pill");
    if (statusPill) {
      statusPill.textContent = state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing" : "Ready";
    }

    const submitButton = document.getElementById("usage-apply-button");
    if (submitButton) {
      submitButton.textContent = state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing..." : "Apply Filters";
      submitButton.disabled = Boolean(state.usage.loading);
    }

    const errorHost = document.getElementById("usage-error-host");
    if (errorHost) {
      errorHost.innerHTML = state.usage.error
        ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.usage.error)}</div>`
        : "";
    }

    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-since", defaultString(filters.since, "30d"));
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-root", defaultString(filters.root, "all"));
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-activity", filters.activity || "");
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-phase", filters.phase || "");
    syncUsageFilterControl("usage-filter-model", filters.model || "");
  }

  function renderRepoOnboardingPanel() {
    const host = document.getElementById("global-repo-onboard");
    if (!host) return;
    const onboarding = state.repoOnboarding || defaultRepoOnboardingState();
    const draft = onboarding.draft || defaultRepoOnboardingState().draft;
    const repoCount = sortedRepos().length;
    const summaryCopy = repoCount
      ? "Add another GitHub repo to the workspace. Advanced routing and scout policies stay editable in the repo Config tab."
      : "No repos are onboarded yet. Add an owner/repo slug or GitHub repo URL to start managing it from this workspace.";
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>Onboard Repo</h3>
          <p>${escapeHTML(summaryCopy)}</p>
        </div>
        <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(repoCount ? `${repoCount} live` : "No repos")}</span>
      </div>
      ${onboarding.error ? `<div id="repo-onboard-error" class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(onboarding.error)}</div>` : `<div id="repo-onboard-error"></div>`}
      <form id="repo-onboard-form" class="config-form">
        <div class="config-grid">
          <label class="selector config-field-wide">
            <span>Repo Slug</span>
            <input id="repo-onboard-slug" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(draft.repo_slug || "")}" placeholder="owner/repo or https://github.com/owner/repo" data-repo-onboard-field="repo_slug" />
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Repo Mode</span>
            <select data-repo-onboard-field="repo_mode">
              ${["local", "fork", "repo", "disabled"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(draft.repo_mode, "local") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(value)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Issue Pick</span>
            <select data-repo-onboard-field="issue_pick_mode">
              ${["manual", "label", "auto"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(draft.issue_pick_mode, "manual") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(value)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>PR Forward</span>
            <select data-repo-onboard-field="pr_forward_mode">
              ${["approve", "auto"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(draft.pr_forward_mode, "approve") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(value)}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
        </div>
        <div class="config-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${onboarding.submitting ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(onboarding.submitting ? "Onboarding..." : "Onboard Repo")}</button>
        </div>
      </form>
    `;
  }

  function submitRepoOnboarding() {
    const payload = repoOnboardingPayload();
    if (!payload.repo_slug) {
      state.repoOnboarding.error = "Enter an owner/repo slug or GitHub repo URL.";
      renderRepoOnboardingPanel();
      toast("warning", "Repo slug required", "Use owner/repo or a GitHub repo URL.");
      return;
    }
    state.repoOnboarding.submitting = true;
    state.repoOnboarding.error = "";
    renderRepoOnboardingPanel();
    api("/api/v1/repos", {
      method: "POST",
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    }).then((response) => {
      const repo = response.repo || null;
      const created = Boolean(response.created);
      state.repoOnboarding = defaultRepoOnboardingState();
      if (repo && repo.repo_slug) {
        applySelectedRepoPayload(repo);
        openRepoView(repo.repo_slug, "config");
      }
      loadOverview({ silent: true });
      toast(created ? "success" : "warning", created ? "Repo onboarded" : "Repo already onboarded", repo && repo.repo_slug ? repo.repo_slug : payload.repo_slug);
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.repoOnboarding.submitting = false;
      state.repoOnboarding.error = error.message;
      if (state.currentView === "home") {
        renderRepoOnboardingPanel();
      }
      toast("danger", "Repo onboarding failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function renderRepoCards(target, repos) {
    const host = document.getElementById(target);
    if (!host) return;
    if (!repos.length) {
      host.innerHTML = buildInlineNotice("No repo overview is available yet.");
      return;
    }
    host.innerHTML = `<div class="repo-card-grid">${repos.map((repo) => {
      return `
        <article class="repo-card">
          <div class="repo-card-title-row">
            <div>
              <h3 class="repo-card-title">${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}</h3>
              <p class="repo-card-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "unknown"))} repo mode · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "unknown"))} issue pick</p>
            </div>
            <span class="mini-count">${pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug).length}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="repo-card-metrics">
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Queued</span>
              <strong>${repo.issue_counts.queued || 0}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Blocked</span>
              <strong>${repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Service</span>
              <strong>${(repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) + (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0)}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Scouts</span>
              <strong>${repoScoutQueueCount(repo)}</strong>
            </div>
            <div class="repo-card-metric">
              <span>Dismissed</span>
              <strong>${repoDismissedScoutCount(repo)}</strong>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="repo-card-actions">
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary repo-card-button" type="button" data-open-repo="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}">Open Repo</button>
            ${repoDismissedScoutCount(repo) > 0 ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary repo-card-button" type="button" data-open-repo="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}" data-open-repo-tab="scouts">Open Scouts</button>` : ""}
          </div>
        </article>
      `;
    }).join("")}</div>`;
  }

  function renderGlobalPage() {
    const attentionItems = filteredAttentionItems();
    const runs = pendingRuns();

        emptyMessage: "No queued or paused work items are waiting.",
      });
    }
    document.getElementById("hud-json").textContent = JSON.stringify(state.overview.hud || {}, null, 2);
  }

  function renderUsagePage() {
    const report = state.usage.report;
    const summary = report ? report.summary || {} : null;
    const totals = summary && summary.totals ? summary.totals : null;
    const inputSide = totals ? Number(totals.input_tokens || 0) + Number(totals.cached_input_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const outputSide = totals ? Number(totals.output_tokens || 0) + Number(totals.reasoning_output_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const inputShare = totals && Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) > 0 ? (inputSide * 100) / Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const outputShare = totals && Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) > 0 ? (outputSide * 100) / Number(totals.total_tokens || 0) : 0;
    const filters = state.usage.filters || defaultUsageState().filters;
    const draftScope = usageFiltersDraftScope();

    ensureBodyStructure("usage", `
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Usage Filters</h3>
            <p>Focus the charts by time window, root, activity, phase, or model.</p>
          </div>
          <span id="usage-status-pill" class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(state.usage.loading ? "Refreshing" : "Ready")}</span>
        </div>
        <form id="usage-filters-form" class="usage-filter-form" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
          <div class="config-grid usage-filter-grid">
            <label class="selector config-selector">
              <span>Since</span>
              <select id="usage-filter-since">
                ${[
                  { value: "24h", label: "24 hours" },
                  { value: "7d", label: "7 days" },
                  { value: "30d", label: "30 days" },

        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Top Sessions</h3>
            <p>Most expensive sessions in the current filtered scope.</p>
          </div>
          <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(report && Array.isArray(report.top_sessions) ? String(report.top_sessions.length) : "0")} rows</span>
        </div>
        <div id="usage-sessions-grid"></div>
      </section>
    `);

    syncUsagePageState(filters);

    document.getElementById("usage-metrics").innerHTML = buildMetricCards([
      { label: "Total Tokens", value: formatTokenCompact(totals && totals.total_tokens || 0), note: "All token spend in the current filter scope." },
      { label: "Sessions", value: String(totals && totals.sessions || 0), note: "Sessions that matched the current filters." },
      { label: "Roots Scanned", value: String(summary && summary.session_roots_scanned || 0), note: "Distinct session trees inspected for this report." },
      { label: "Input Share", value: formatPercent(inputShare), note: "Input plus cached-input percentage of total tokens." },
      { label: "Output Tokens", value: formatTokenCompact(outputSide), note: "Output plus reasoning-output token total." },
      { label: "Missing Telemetry", value: String(totals && totals.missing_telemetry || 0), note: "Sessions with no token_count snapshots." },
    ]);

    renderUsageChart("usage-root-chart", {
      type: "donut",
      height: 300,
      title: "Tokens by root",
      legend: { position: "right" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData(report ? report.by_root : [], 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading usage breakdown..." : "No root data is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-phase-chart", {
      type: "donut",
      height: 300,
      title: "Tokens by phase",
      legend: { position: "right" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData(report ? report.by_phase : [], 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading phase data..." : "No phase data is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-activity-chart", {
      type: "bar",
      height: 320,
      title: "Tokens by activity",
      xAxis: { title: "Activity" },
      yAxis: { title: "Tokens" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData(report ? report.by_activity : [], 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading activity data..." : "No activity data is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-day-chart", {
      type: "area",
      height: 320,
      title: "Daily token trend",
      xAxis: { title: "Day" },
      yAxis: { title: "Tokens" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageDayChartData(report ? report.by_day : []) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading trend data..." : "No daily trend is available.");

    renderUsageChart("usage-lane-chart", {
      type: "bar",
      height: 320,
      title: "Top lanes",
      xAxis: { title: "Lane" },
      yAxis: { title: "Tokens" },
      series: [{ name: "Tokens", data: usageGroupChartData((report ? report.by_lane : []).filter((item) => defaultString(item.key, "") !== "(unknown)"), 8) }],
    }, state.usage.loading ? "Loading lane data..." : "No lane data is available.");

    const insightsHost = document.getElementById("usage-insights");
    if (insightsHost) {
      insightsHost.innerHTML = usageInsightsMarkup(report ? report.insights : []);
    }

    renderGrid("usage-sessions-grid", [
      { field: "session_id", label: "Session" },
      { field: "root", label: "Root" },
      { field: "activity", label: "Activity" },
      { field: "phase", label: "Phase" },
      { field: "lane", label: "Lane" },
      { field: "model", label: "Model" },
      { field: "total_tokens", label: "Tokens", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(formatTokenCompact(row.total_tokens))}</span>` },
      { field: "timestamp", label: "Updated", render: (row) => `<span class="data-value-text">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(row.timestamp))}</span>` },
      { field: "cwd", label: "Workspace" },
    ], (report && report.top_sessions || []).map((session) => ({
      session_id: defaultString(session.session_id, "(unknown)"),
      root: defaultString(session.root, "(unknown)"),
      activity: defaultString(session.activity, "(unknown)"),
      phase: defaultString(session.phase, "(unknown)"),
      lane: defaultString(session.lane, "(unknown)"),
      model: defaultString(session.model, "(unknown)"),
      total_tokens: Number(session.total_tokens || 0),
      timestamp: defaultString(session.timestamp, ""),
      cwd: defaultString(session.cwd, "(unknown)"),
    })), {
      maxHeight: "420px",
      emptyMessage: state.usage.loading ? "Loading top sessions..." : defaultString(state.usage.error, "No sessions matched these usage filters."),
    });
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, document.getElementById("usage-filters-form"));
  }

  function filteredIssueQueueItems() {
    const filter = filterState("issues");
    return (state.issueQueue.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["title", "repo_slug", "source_url", "triage_rationale", "blocked_reason"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredInvestigations() {
    const filter = filterState("investigations");
    return (state.investigations.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["query", "repo_slug", "overall_short_explanation", "run_id", "pause_reason", "pause_until"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredWorkRuns() {
    const filter = filterState("work");
    return sortRuns(state.overview ? state.overview.work_runs || [] : []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesKindFilter(item, filter.kind) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["repo_slug", "run_id", "target_url", "current_phase", "status", "backend", "pause_reason", "pause_until"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredFeedbackItems() {
    const filter = filterState("feedback");
    const sourceItems = state.feedbackTab === "reviews" ? state.feedback.reviews : state.feedback.replies;
    return (sourceItems || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["subject", "repo_slug", "draft_summary", "draft_body", "target_url", "comment_path", "pause_reason", "pause_until"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredApprovalItems() {
    const filter = filterState("approvals");
    return (state.approvals.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesKindFilter(item, filter.kind) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["subject", "repo_slug", "reason", "next_action", "target_url"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function filteredAttentionItems() {
    const filter = filterState("attention");
    return (state.attention.items || []).filter((item) => {
      return matchesRepoFilter(item, filter.repo) &&
        matchesAttentionFilter(item, filter.attention) &&
        matchesKindFilter(item, filter.kind) &&
        matchesQuery(item, ["summary", "reason", "detail", "repo_slug", "target_url", "kind", "subtype", "severity", "path", "route"], filter.query);
    });
  }

  function selectedAttentionItemIDs() {
    return (state.attention.selectedItemIDs || []).filter((itemID) => state.attention.items.some((item) => item.id === itemID));
  }

  function selectedAttentionItems() {
    const selected = new Set(selectedAttentionItemIDs());
    return filteredAttentionItems().filter((item) => selected.has(item.id));
  }

  function visibleAttentionItemIDs() {
    return filteredAttentionItems().map((item) => String(item.id || "")).filter(Boolean);
  }

  function toggleAttentionItemSelection(itemID, checked) {
    const next = new Set(selectedAttentionItemIDs());
    if (checked) {
      next.add(itemID);
    } else {
      next.delete(itemID);
    }
    setSelectedAttentionItemIDs(Array.from(next));
  }

  function selectAllVisibleAttentionItems() {
    setSelectedAttentionItemIDs(visibleAttentionItemIDs());
  }

  function clearAttentionSelection() {
    setSelectedAttentionItemIDs([]);
    state.attention.bulkAction = "";
  }

  function clearAttentionDetail() {
    state.attention.detailItemID = "";
    state.attention.detailData = null;
    state.attention.detailError = "";
    state.attention.detailLoading = false;
  }

  function attentionItemByID(itemID) {
    return (state.attention.items || []).find((item) => item.id === itemID) || null;
  }

  function attentionDetailItem() {
    if (state.attention.detailData && state.attention.detailData.item) {
      return state.attention.detailData.item;
    }
    if (!state.attention.detailItemID) return null;
    return attentionItemByID(state.attention.detailItemID);
  }

  function attentionDetailActions() {
    return Array.isArray(state.attention.detailData && state.attention.detailData.actions)
      ? state.attention.detailData.actions
      : [];
  }

  function applyAttentionDetailPayload(payload) {
    state.attention.detailData = payload || null;
    state.attention.detailItemID = defaultString(payload && payload.item && payload.item.id, state.attention.detailItemID);
    state.attention.detailLoading = false;
    state.attention.detailError = "";
  }

  function loadAttentionDetail(itemID, options = {}) {
    const id = String(itemID || "").trim();
    if (!id) {
      clearAttentionDetail();
      if (state.currentView === "home" && state.overview) {
        renderAttentionInbox();
      }
      return Promise.resolve(null);
    }
    state.attention.detailItemID = id;
    state.attention.detailLoading = true;
    if (!options.silent) {
      state.attention.detailError = "";
    }
    if (state.currentView === "home" && state.overview) {
      renderAttentionInbox();
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/attention/items/${encodeURIComponent(id)}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.attention.detailItemID !== id) return payload;
      applyAttentionDetailPayload(payload);
      if (state.currentView === "home" && state.overview) {
        renderAttentionInbox();
      }
      return payload;
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.attention.detailItemID !== id) throw error;
      state.attention.detailLoading = false;
      state.attention.detailError = error.message;
      if (options.allowMissing) {
        clearAttentionDetail();
      }
      if (state.currentView === "home" && state.overview) {
        renderAttentionInbox();
      }
      if (!options.silent && !options.allowMissing) {
        toast("danger", "Attention detail failed", error.message);
      }
      throw error;
    });
  }

  function openAttentionItem(item) {
    if (!item || !item.id) return;
    loadAttentionDetail(item.id, { silent: true }).catch(() => {});
  }

  function focusAttentionTile(itemID) {
    const id = String(itemID || "").trim();
    if (!id) return;
    window.setTimeout(() => {
      const tile = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll("[data-attention-tile]"))
        .find((entry) => entry.getAttribute("data-attention-tile") === id);
      if (tile) {
        tile.focus();
      }
    }, 0);
  }

  function attentionDisplayTitle(item) {
    const summary = defaultString(item && item.summary, item && item.id);
    const repoPrefix = defaultString(item && item.repo_slug, "");
    if (repoPrefix && summary.startsWith(`${repoPrefix}: `)) {
      return summary.slice(repoPrefix.length + 2);
    }
    return summary;
  }

  function attentionStatusLabel(item) {
    if (!item) return "Queued";
    if (item.kind === "finding") {
      return findingStatusLabel(item.status);
    }
    if (item.kind === "import_candidate") {
      return defaultString(item.import_candidate_status, "candidate").replace(/_/g, " ");
    }
    return defaultString(item.status, defaultString(item.attention_state, "queued")).replace(/_/g, " ");
  }

  function attentionKindLabel(kind) {
    switch (String(kind || "").trim()) {
      case "approval":
        return "Approval";
      case "finding":
        return "Finding";
      case "import_candidate":
        return "Import Candidate";
      case "work_run":
        return "Run";
      case "work_item":
        return "Work Item";
      case "investigation":
        return "Task";
      case "issue":
        return "Issue";
      default:
        return defaultString(kind, "Attention");
    }
  }

  function attentionSubtypeLabel(subtype) {
    const normalized = String(subtype || "").trim();
    if (!normalized) return "";
    switch (normalized) {
      case "work_item":
        return "Draft";
      case "planned_item":
        return "Planned Work";
      case "scout_job":
        return "Scout Job";
      case "work_run":
        return "Run Gate";
      case "manual_import":
        return "Manual Import";
      default:
        return normalized.replace(/_/g, " ");
    }
  }

  function itemSupportsAttentionAction(item, action) {
    if (!item || !action) return false;
    const actions = Array.isArray(item.available_actions) ? item.available_actions : [];
    return actions.includes(action) || defaultString(item.action_kind, "") === action;
  }

  function attentionPrimaryAction(item) {
    if (!item) return "";
    const preferred = [
      defaultString(item.action_kind, ""),
      "approve_work_item",
      "approve_planned_item",
      "investigate_issue",
      "review_on_github",
      "retry_scout_job",
      "resolve_run",
      "sync_run",
      "requeue_work_item",
      "promote_finding",
      "promote_import_candidate",
      "open_investigation",
      "open_work_item",
      "open_run",
      "open_issue",
    ].filter(Boolean);
    return preferred.find((action) => itemSupportsAttentionAction(item, action)) || "";
  }

  function attentionSecondaryAction(item, primaryAction) {
    if (!item) return "";
    const primary = defaultString(primaryAction, "");
    return [
      "launch_issue_work",
      "dismiss_finding",
      "drop_import_candidate",
      "drop_approval",
      "drop_run",
      "drop_work_item",
    ].find((action) => action !== primary && itemSupportsAttentionAction(item, action)) || "";
  }

  function attentionActionLabel(action) {
    switch (action) {
      case "approve_work_item":
        return "Approve Drafts";
      case "approve_planned_item":
        return "Launch Planned Work";
      case "retry_scout_job":
        return "Retry Scouts";
      case "resolve_run":
        return "Resolve Runs";
      case "sync_run":
        return "Refresh Runs";
      case "promote_finding":
        return "Promote Findings";
      case "dismiss_finding":
        return "Dismiss Findings";
      case "promote_import_candidate":
        return "Promote Import Candidates";
      case "drop_import_candidate":
        return "Drop Import Candidates";
      case "drop_approval":
        return "Drop Approval Items";
      case "submit_work_item":
        return "Submit Work Items";
      case "requeue_work_item":
        return "Requeue Work Items";
      case "run_work_item":
        return "Run Work Items";
      case "fix_work_item":
        return "Revise Drafts";
      case "drop_work_item":
        return "Drop Work Items";
      case "restore_work_item":
        return "Restore Work Items";
      case "investigate_issue":
        return "Investigate Issues";
      case "launch_issue_work":
        return "Start Work";
      case "save_issue":
        return "Save Issue";
      case "clear_issue_schedule":
        return "Clear Schedule";
      case "save_finding":
        return "Save Finding";
      case "save_import_candidate":
        return "Save Candidate";
      case "drop_run":
        return "Drop Runs";
      case "review_on_github":
        return "Review on GitHub";
      case "open_work_item":
        return "Open Work Item";
      case "open_run":
        return "Open Run";
      case "open_issue":
        return "Open Issue";
      case "open_investigation":
        return "Open Task";
      case "open_finding":
        return "Open Finding";
      case "open_import_candidate":
        return "Open Import";
      default:
        return defaultString(action, "Apply");
    }
  }

  function attentionActionButtonLabel(action) {
    switch (action) {
      case "approve_work_item":
        return "Approve";
      case "approve_planned_item":
        return "Launch";
      case "submit_work_item":
        return "Submit";
      case "retry_scout_job":
        return "Retry";
      case "resolve_run":
        return "Resolve";
      case "sync_run":
        return "Refresh";
      case "investigate_issue":
        return "Investigate";
      case "launch_issue_work":
        return "Start Work";
      case "promote_finding":
      case "promote_import_candidate":
        return "Promote";
      case "save_issue":
      case "save_finding":
      case "save_import_candidate":
        return "Save";
      case "run_work_item":
        return "Run";
      case "fix_work_item":
        return "Revise";
      case "dismiss_finding":
      case "drop_import_candidate":
      case "drop_approval":
      case "drop_run":
      case "drop_work_item":
        return "Drop";
      case "requeue_work_item":
        return "Requeue";
      case "restore_work_item":
        return "Restore";
      case "review_on_github":
        return "Review";
      default:
        return attentionActionLabel(action);
    }
  }

  function attentionActionTone(action) {
    switch (action) {
      case "approve_work_item":
      case "approve_planned_item":
      case "submit_work_item":
      case "retry_scout_job":
      case "resolve_run":
      case "investigate_issue":
      case "launch_issue_work":
      case "promote_finding":
      case "promote_import_candidate":
      case "save_issue":
      case "save_finding":
      case "save_import_candidate":
        return "primary";
      default:
        return "secondary";
    }
  }

  function attentionActionIsDestructive(action) {
    return action === "dismiss_finding" ||
      action === "drop_import_candidate" ||
      action === "drop_approval" ||
      action === "drop_run" ||
      action === "drop_work_item";
  }

  function attentionActionCount(items, action) {
    return (items || []).filter((item) => itemSupportsAttentionAction(item, action)).length;
  }

  function attentionBulkActionOptions(items) {
    const actions = [
      "approve_work_item",
      "approve_planned_item",
      "retry_scout_job",
      "resolve_run",
      "sync_run",
      "promote_finding",
      "dismiss_finding",
      "promote_import_candidate",
      "drop_import_candidate",
      "drop_approval",
      "requeue_work_item",
    ];
    return actions.map((action) => ({
      value: action,
      count: attentionActionCount(items, action),
      label: attentionActionLabel(action),
    })).filter((option) => option.count > 0);
  }

  function renderAttentionActionButton(item, action, className) {
    if (!item || !action) return "";
    return `<button class="${escapeHTML(className)}" type="button" data-attention-action="${escapeHTML(action)}" data-attention-item-id="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">${escapeHTML(attentionActionButtonLabel(action))}</button>`;
  }

  function attentionGroupMode() {
    return defaultString(state.attention.groupBy, "attention_state");
  }

  function attentionGroupOptionLabel(value) {
    switch (value) {
      case "attention_state":
        return "State";
      case "kind":
        return "Kind";
      case "repo":
        return "Repo";
      default:
        return defaultString(value, "State");
    }
  }

  function attentionLaneLabel(groupBy, key) {
    if (groupBy === "kind") {
      return attentionKindLabel(key);
    }
    if (groupBy === "repo") {
      return key ? key : "Workspace";
    }
    switch (key) {
      case "failed":
        return "Failed";
      case "blocked":
        return "Blocked";
      case "queued":
        return "Queued";
      case "active":
        return "Active";
      case "completed":
        return "Completed";
      default:
        return defaultString(key, "Inbox");
    }
  }

  function attentionLaneKey(item, groupBy) {
    if (groupBy === "kind") {
      return defaultString(item && item.kind, "attention");
    }
    if (groupBy === "repo") {
      return defaultString(item && item.repo_slug, "");
    }
    return defaultString(item && item.attention_state, "queued");
  }

  function groupedAttentionLanes(items) {
    const groupBy = attentionGroupMode();
    const groups = new Map();
    const order = [];
    const ensureGroup = (key) => {
      if (!groups.has(key)) {
        groups.set(key, []);
        order.push(key);
      }
    };
    if (groupBy === "attention_state") {
      ["failed", "blocked", "queued", "active", "completed"].forEach(ensureGroup);
    }
    items.forEach((item) => {
      const key = attentionLaneKey(item, groupBy);
      ensureGroup(key);
      groups.get(key).push(item);
    });
    const keys = order.filter((key) => {
      if (groupBy === "attention_state") {
        return groups.get(key).length > 0 || key === "failed" || key === "blocked" || key === "queued";
      }
      return groups.get(key).length > 0;
    }).sort((left, right) => {
      if (groupBy === "kind") {
        const rank = {
          approval: 0,
          finding: 1,
          import_candidate: 2,
          work_run: 3,
          work_item: 4,
          investigation: 5,
          issue: 6,
        };
        return (rank[left] ?? 99) - (rank[right] ?? 99) || String(left).localeCompare(String(right));
      }
      if (groupBy === "repo") {
        if (!left && right) return -1;
        if (left && !right) return 1;
        return String(left).localeCompare(String(right));
      }
      const rank = {
        failed: 0,
        blocked: 1,
        queued: 2,
        active: 3,
        completed: 4,
      };
      return (rank[left] ?? 99) - (rank[right] ?? 99);
    });
    return keys.map((key) => ({
      key,
      label: attentionLaneLabel(groupBy, key),
      items: groups.get(key) || [],
    }));
  }

  function attentionVisibleStateCounts(items) {
    const counts = { failed: 0, blocked: 0, queued: 0 };
    (items || []).forEach((item) => {
      const key = defaultString(item.attention_state, "queued");
      if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(counts, key)) {
        counts[key] += 1;
      }
    });
    return counts;
  }

  function renderAttentionTile(item, laneKey) {
    const selectedIDs = new Set(selectedAttentionItemIDs());
    const selected = selectedIDs.has(item.id);
    const opened = state.attention.detailItemID === item.id;
    const primaryAction = attentionPrimaryAction(item);
    const secondaryAction = attentionSecondaryAction(item, primaryAction);
    const subtitle = attentionSubtypeLabel(item.subtype);
    const detail = defaultString(item.detail, defaultString(item.target_url, defaultString(item.path, item.route)));
    return `
      <article class="attention-tile attention-state-${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.attention_state, "queued"))} ${selected ? "attention-tile-selected" : ""} ${opened ? "attention-tile-open" : ""}" tabindex="0" data-attention-tile="${escapeHTML(item.id)}" data-attention-lane="${escapeHTML(laneKey)}">
        <div class="attention-tile-head">
          <label class="attention-tile-check">
            <input type="checkbox" data-attention-toggle="${escapeHTML(item.id)}" ${selected ? "checked" : ""} />
            <span>Select</span>
          </label>
          <div class="attention-tile-pills">
            <span class="status-pill attention-kind-pill">${escapeHTML(attentionKindLabel(item.kind))}</span>
            ${renderStatePill(defaultString(item.attention_state, "queued"), attentionStatusLabel(item))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="attention-tile-copy">
          <p class="attention-tile-repo">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.repo_slug, "Workspace"))}${subtitle ? ` · ${escapeHTML(subtitle)}` : ""}</p>
          <h3>${escapeHTML(attentionDisplayTitle(item))}</h3>
          <p class="attention-tile-reason">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.reason, "(no summary)"))}</p>
          ${detail && detail !== item.reason ? `<p class="attention-tile-detail">${escapeHTML(detail)}</p>` : ""}
        </div>
        <div class="attention-tile-meta">
          ${item.severity ? `<span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.severity, ""))}</span>` : ""}
          ${item.path ? `<span>${escapeHTML(item.path)}</span>` : ""}
          ${item.updated_at ? `<span>${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at))}</span>` : ""}
        </div>
        <div class="attention-tile-actions">
          ${primaryAction ? renderAttentionActionButton(item, primaryAction, `tx-btn tx-btn-${attentionActionTone(primaryAction)} tx-btn-sm`) : ""}
          ${secondaryAction ? renderAttentionActionButton(item, secondaryAction, `tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm${attentionActionIsDestructive(secondaryAction) ? " attention-btn-danger" : ""}`) : ""}
        </div>
      </article>
    `;
  }

  function attentionDetailButton(item, action, extra = {}) {
    if (!item || !action) return "";
    const tone = extra.tone || attentionActionTone(action);
    const destructive = attentionActionIsDestructive(action);
    const className = extra.className || `tx-btn tx-btn-${tone}${extra.small ? " tx-btn-sm" : ""}${destructive ? " attention-btn-danger" : ""}`;
    return `<button class="${escapeHTML(className)}" type="button" data-attention-detail-action="${escapeHTML(action)}" data-attention-detail-item-id="${escapeHTML(item.id)}" ${extra.disabled ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(extra.label || attentionActionButtonLabel(action))}</button>`;
  }

  function attentionIssueActionPayload() {
    const scheduleInput = document.getElementById("attention-issue-schedule");
    const deferredInput = document.getElementById("attention-issue-deferred");
    const priorityInput = document.getElementById("attention-issue-priority");
    const scheduleValue = scheduleInput ? String(scheduleInput.value || "") : "";
    return {
      priority: priorityInput ? Number.parseInt(String(priorityInput.value || "3"), 10) : 3,
      schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(scheduleValue),
      deferred_reason: deferredInput ? String(deferredInput.value || "") : "",
      clear_schedule: !scheduleValue,
    };
  }

  function attentionFindingActionPayload() {
    return {
      title: String(document.getElementById("attention-finding-title") && document.getElementById("attention-finding-title").value || "").trim(),
      summary: String(document.getElementById("attention-finding-summary") && document.getElementById("attention-finding-summary").value || "").trim(),
      detail: String(document.getElementById("attention-finding-detail") && document.getElementById("attention-finding-detail").value || "").trim(),
      evidence: String(document.getElementById("attention-finding-evidence") && document.getElementById("attention-finding-evidence").value || "").trim(),
      severity: String(document.getElementById("attention-finding-severity") && document.getElementById("attention-finding-severity").value || "medium").trim(),
      work_type: String(document.getElementById("attention-finding-work-type") && document.getElementById("attention-finding-work-type").value || "feature").trim(),
    };
  }

  function attentionImportCandidateActionPayload() {
    return {
      title: String(document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-title") && document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-title").value || "").trim(),
      summary: String(document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-summary") && document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-summary").value || "").trim(),
      detail: String(document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-detail") && document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-detail").value || "").trim(),
      evidence: String(document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-evidence") && document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-evidence").value || "").trim(),
      severity: String(document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-severity") && document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-severity").value || "medium").trim(),
      work_type: String(document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-work-type") && document.getElementById("attention-import-candidate-work-type").value || "feature").trim(),
    };
  }

  function attentionWorkItemFixPayload() {
    return {
      instruction: String(document.getElementById("attention-work-item-fix-instruction") && document.getElementById("attention-work-item-fix-instruction").value || "").trim(),
    };
  }

  function attentionActionPayload(action) {
    switch (action) {
      case "save_issue":
        return attentionIssueActionPayload();
      case "save_finding":
        return attentionFindingActionPayload();
      case "save_import_candidate":
        return attentionImportCandidateActionPayload();
      case "fix_work_item":
        return attentionWorkItemFixPayload();
      default:
        return null;
    }
  }

  function performAttentionActionRequest(item, action, payload) {
    if (action === "review_on_github") {
      if (item.target_url) {
        window.open(item.target_url, "_blank", "noopener");
        return Promise.resolve({ item });
      }
      return Promise.reject(new Error("external review URL is missing"));
    }
    if (action.startsWith("open_")) {
      openAttentionItem(item);
      return Promise.resolve({ item });
    }
    return api(`/api/v1/attention/items/${encodeURIComponent(item.id)}/actions/${encodeURIComponent(action)}`, {
      method: "POST",
      body: payload ? JSON.stringify(payload) : undefined,
    });
  }

  function attentionActionSuccessCopy(action, successCount, failureCount) {
    if (failureCount) {
      return `${successCount} updated, ${failureCount} failed.`;
    }
    return `${successCount} item${successCount === 1 ? "" : "s"} updated.`;
  }

  function executeAttentionAction(action, items, options = {}) {
    const applicableItems = (items || []).filter((item) => options.ignoreSummary || itemSupportsAttentionAction(item, action));
    if (!applicableItems.length) {
      toast("warning", "Action unavailable", "No selected tiles support that action.");
      return;
    }

    const run = () => {
      if (applicableItems.length === 1) {
        const item = applicableItems[0];
        const payload = options.payload || attentionActionPayload(action);
        if (action === "review_on_github" || action.startsWith("open_")) {
          performAttentionActionRequest(item, action, payload).catch((error) => {
            toast("danger", `${attentionActionLabel(action)} failed`, error.message);
          });
          return;
        }
        performAttentionActionRequest(item, action, payload).then((response) => {
          const nextDetailID = response && response.item && response.item.id ? response.item.id : item.id;
          if (response && response.item) {
            state.attention.detailData = {
              item: response.item,
              detail: response.detail || null,
              actions: attentionDetailActions(),
            };
          } else if (state.attention.detailItemID === item.id && !action.startsWith("open_") && action !== "review_on_github") {
            clearAttentionDetail();
          }
          Promise.allSettled([
            load(),
            response && response.item ? loadAttentionDetail(nextDetailID, { silent: true }) : Promise.resolve(),
          ]).then(() => {
            toast("success", attentionActionLabel(action), attentionActionSuccessCopy(action, 1, 0));
          });
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", `${attentionActionLabel(action)} failed`, error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      api("/api/v1/attention/batch", {
        method: "POST",
        body: JSON.stringify({
          action,
          item_ids: applicableItems.map((item) => item.id),
        }),
      }).then((payload) => {
        clearAttentionSelection();
        Promise.allSettled([load()]).then(() => {
          toast(payload.failure_count ? "warning" : "success", attentionActionLabel(action), attentionActionSuccessCopy(action, payload.success_count || 0, payload.failure_count || 0));
        });
      }).catch((error) => {
        toast("danger", `${attentionActionLabel(action)} failed`, error.message);
      });
    };

    const confirmation = attentionActionConfirmation(action, applicableItems.length);
    if (confirmation) {
      requestConfirmation({
        title: confirmation.title,
        message: confirmation.message,
        confirmLabel: confirmation.confirmLabel,
        tone: confirmation.tone,
        onConfirm: run,
      });
      return;
    }
    run();
  }

  function renderAttentionIssueDetailPane(item, detail) {
    const issue = detail && detail.issue ? detail.issue : null;
    if (!issue) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Issue detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    return `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(issue.repo_slug)} #${escapeHTML(issue.source_number)}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(issue.title)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.source_url, "No source URL captured."))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Priority</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(issue.priority_label)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(issue.work_type))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(issue.attention_state, issue.status)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Triage</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.triage_status, "-"))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        ${attentionDetailButton(item, "investigate_issue")}
        ${attentionDetailButton(item, "launch_issue_work")}
      </div>
      <div class="config-grid">
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Priority</span>
          <select id="attention-issue-priority">
            ${[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => `<option value="${priority}" ${issue.priority === priority ? "selected" : ""}>P${priority}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Schedule</span>
          <input id="attention-issue-schedule" type="datetime-local" value="${escapeHTML(toDateTimeLocal(issue.schedule_at))}" />
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Deferred Reason</span>
          <textarea id="attention-issue-deferred" rows="3">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.deferred_reason, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
      </div>
      <div class="config-actions">
        ${attentionDetailButton(item, "clear_issue_schedule", { tone: "secondary" })}
        ${attentionDetailButton(item, "save_issue")}
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Schedule</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(issue.schedule_at) : "", "Not scheduled"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Triage Rationale</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.triage_rationale, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Blocked Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.blocked_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Run</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.last_run_id, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Published PR</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.published_pr_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
    `;
  }

      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderAttentionWorkRunDetailPane(item, detail, options = {}) {
    const runDetail = detail && detail.run ? detail.run : null;
    const logs = detail && detail.logs ? detail.logs : null;
    if (!runDetail || !runDetail.summary) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Run detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    const summary = runDetail.summary;
    const logTail = logs && logs.tail_content ? logs.tail_content : "No log content available.";
    const pauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason);
    const toolbarButtons = [];
    if (options.reviewURL) {
      toolbarButtons.push(attentionDetailButton(item, "review_on_github", { tone: "secondary" }));
    }
    if (runDetail.resolve_allowed) {
      toolbarButtons.push(attentionDetailButton(item, "resolve_run", { tone: "secondary" }));
    }
    if (runDetail.sync_allowed) {
      toolbarButtons.push(attentionDetailButton(item, "sync_run", { tone: "secondary" }));
    }
    toolbarButtons.push(attentionDetailButton(item, options.dropAction || "drop_run", { tone: "secondary" }));
    return `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">Run</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.run_id, item.run_id))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(runRepoDisplay(summary))} · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.backend, "unknown"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(summary.attention_state, "active"), defaultString(summary.status, "active"), summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Phase</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.current_phase, "(none)"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Next Action</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(runDetail.next_action, "(none)"))}</span></div>
          ${pauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(pauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">${toolbarButtons.join("")}</div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Run State</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.target_url, "No target URL recorded."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Target</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.target_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Publication</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.publication_state, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Human Gate</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(runDetail.human_gate_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Log Path</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(logs && logs.tail_path, defaultString(logs && logs.default_path, "(none)")))}</p></article>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Log Tail</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(logs && logs.artifact_root, "No artifact root available."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(logTail)}</pre>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderAttentionWorkItemDetailPane(item, detail, options = {}) {
    const workItem = detail && detail.work_item ? detail.work_item.item : null;
    const detailData = detail && detail.work_item ? detail.work_item : null;
    if (!workItem || !detailData) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Work item detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    const draft = workItem.latest_draft || null;
    const pauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(workItem.pause_until, workItem.pause_reason);
    const events = (detailData.events || []).map((event) => `
      <li>
        <strong>${escapeHTML(event.event_type)}</strong>
        <span>${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(event.created_at))}</span>
        <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(event.actor, "-"))}</span>
      </li>
    `).join("");
    return `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(workItem.repo_slug, "Standalone"))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(workItem.subject, workItem.id))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(workItem.target_url, "No external target recorded."))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(item.attention_state, "active"), defaultString(workItem.status, "-"), workItem.pause_until, workItem.pause_reason)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Linked Run</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(workItem.linked_run_id, "-"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(workItem.updated_at))}</span></div>
          ${pauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(pauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      ${options.showApprovalContext ? `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Approval Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(options.reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Step</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(options.nextAction, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      ` : ""}
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        ${workItem.status === "draft_ready" ? attentionDetailButton(item, options.approvalAction || "submit_work_item") : ""}
        ${workItem.status === "paused" ? attentionDetailButton(item, "requeue_work_item", { tone: "secondary" }) : ""}
        ${attentionDetailButton(item, "fix_work_item", { tone: "secondary", label: "Revise Draft" })}
        ${attentionDetailButton(item, options.dropAction || "drop_work_item", { tone: "secondary" })}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Draft Preview</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft && draft.summary, "No draft is ready yet."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${draft && draft.kind === "review"
          ? renderReviewDraftDetail(draft)
          : renderReplyDraftDetail(workItem, draft)}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Revise Draft</h3>
            <p>Write an instruction for Nana to revise the current draft.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Instruction</span>
          <textarea id="attention-work-item-fix-instruction" rows="4" placeholder="Clarify the justification and tighten the wording."></textarea>
        </label>
        <div class="config-actions">
          ${attentionDetailButton(item, "fix_work_item")}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Events</h3>
            <p>Audit history for this item.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${events ? `<ul class="status-list">${events}</ul>` : '<div class="status-pill">No events are recorded yet.</div>'}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderAttentionInvestigationDetailPane(detail) {
    if (!detail || !detail.summary) {
