      return '<div class="status-pill">Investigation detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    const summary = detail.summary;
    const report = detail.final_report || null;
    const validator = detail.latest_validator_result || null;
    const proofsMarkup = report && Array.isArray(report.overall_proofs) && report.overall_proofs.length
      ? `<ul class="status-list">${report.overall_proofs.map((proof) => `
          <li>
            <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.title, proof.kind))}</strong>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.why_it_proves, "(none)"))}</span>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.path, defaultString(proof.link, "(none)")))}</span>
          </li>
        `).join("")}</ul>`
      : '<div class="status-pill">No proofs are available.</div>';
    const findingsMarkup = report && Array.isArray(report.issues) && report.issues.length
      ? `<div class="queue-summary">${report.issues.map((issue) => `
          <article class="queue-item">
            <span class="queue-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.id, "Issue"))}</span>
            <p class="queue-copy"><strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.short_explanation, "(none)"))}</strong></p>
            <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.detailed_explanation, "(none)"))}</p>
          </article>
        `).join("")}</div>`
      : '<div class="status-pill">No issue-level findings were recorded.</div>';
    const validatorMarkup = validator
      ? `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Accepted</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(Boolean(validator.accepted)))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(validator.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        ${Array.isArray(validator.violations) && validator.violations.length ? `
          <ul class="status-list">${validator.violations.map((violation) => `
            <li>
              <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.code, "violation"))}</strong>
              <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.path, "$"))}</span>
              <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.message, "(none)"))}</span>
            </li>
          `).join("")}</ul>
        ` : '<div class="status-pill">No validator violations.</div>'}
      `
      : '<div class="status-pill">No validator result available.</div>';
    return `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.repo_slug, "Workspace"))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.overall_status, summary.status))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.query, "(no query)"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Run</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Accepted Round</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.accepted_round, "-"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Issues</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.issue_count, 0))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.updated_at))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.overall_short_explanation, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Workspace</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.workspace_root, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Final Report</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.final_report_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Detailed Explanation</h3><p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.completed_at ? formatDateTime(summary.completed_at) : "", "Run not completed yet."))}</p></div></div>
        <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(report && report.overall_detailed_explanation, "(none)"))}</p>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Proofs</h3><p>Primary and supplementary proof links.</p></div></div>
        ${proofsMarkup}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Findings</h3><p>Issue-level conclusions for this investigation.</p></div></div>
        ${findingsMarkup}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Validator</h3><p>Latest validator result for this run.</p></div></div>
        ${validatorMarkup}
      </div>
    `;
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
  }

  function renderAttentionApprovalDetailPane(item, detail) {
    if (!detail) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Approval detail is unavailable.</div>';
    }
    if (detail.work_item) {
      return renderAttentionWorkItemDetailPane(item, detail, {
        showApprovalContext: true,
        reason: detail.reason,
        nextAction: detail.next_action,
        approvalAction: "approve_work_item",
        dropAction: "drop_approval",
      });
    }
    if (detail.work_run) {
      return `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Step</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.next_action, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">External URL</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.external_url, defaultString(detail.target_url, "(none)")))}</p></article>
        </div>
        ${renderAttentionWorkRunDetailPane(item, detail.work_run, {
          dropAction: "drop_approval",
          reviewURL: defaultString(detail.external_url, detail.target_url),
        })}
      `;
    }
    if (detail.planned_item) {
      const plannedItem = detail.planned_item;
      return `
        <div class="drawer-summary">
          <div>
            <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.launch_kind, "planned"))}</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.title, "(untitled)"))}</span>
            <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.description, "(no description)"))}</p>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">State</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(plannedItem.state === "failed" ? "failed" : "queued", plannedItem.state)}</span></div>
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(plannedItem.work_type))}</span></div>
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Priority</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(`P${defaultString(plannedItem.priority, 3)}`)}</span></div>
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Schedule</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(plannedItem.schedule_at) : "", "Ready now"))}</span></div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-toolbar">
          ${attentionDetailButton(item, "approve_planned_item")}
          ${attentionDetailButton(item, "drop_approval", { tone: "secondary" })}
        </div>
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Target URL</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.target_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(plannedItem.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    if (detail.scout_job) {
      const scoutJob = detail.scout_job;
      return `
        <div class="drawer-summary">
          <div>
            <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(scoutJob.role, "scout"))}</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(scoutJob.title, "(untitled)"))}</span>
            <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(scoutJob.summary, "(no summary)"))}</p>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill("failed", defaultString(scoutJob.status, "failed"))}</span></div>
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(scoutJob.work_type))}</span></div>
            <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(scoutJob.updated_at))}</span></div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-toolbar">
          ${attentionDetailButton(item, "retry_scout_job")}
          ${attentionDetailButton(item, "drop_approval", { tone: "secondary" })}
        </div>
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Rationale</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(scoutJob.rationale, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Evidence</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(scoutJob.evidence, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(scoutJob.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
      `;
    }
    return `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Step</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.next_action, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">External URL</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(detail.external_url, defaultString(detail.target_url, "(none)")))}</p></article>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderAttentionDetailPane() {
    const selected = attentionDetailItem();
    if (state.attention.detailLoading && !selected) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Loading detail...</div>';
    }
    if (state.attention.detailError && !selected) {
      return `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.attention.detailError)}</div>`;
    }
    if (!selected) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">Select a tile to inspect it inline.</div>';
    }
    if (state.attention.detailError) {
      return `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.attention.detailError)}</div>`;
    }
    const detail = state.attention.detailData ? state.attention.detailData.detail : null;
    if (selected.kind === "approval") {
      return renderAttentionApprovalDetailPane(selected, detail);
    }
    if (selected.kind === "finding") {
      return renderAttentionFindingDetailPane(selected, detail);
    }
    if (selected.kind === "import_candidate") {
      return renderAttentionImportCandidateDetailPane(selected, detail);
    }
    if (selected.kind === "issue") {
      return renderAttentionIssueDetailPane(selected, detail);
    }
    if (selected.kind === "work_run") {
      return renderAttentionWorkRunDetailPane(selected, detail);
    }
    if (selected.kind === "work_item") {
      return renderAttentionWorkItemDetailPane(selected, detail);
    }
    if (selected.kind === "investigation") {
      return renderAttentionInvestigationDetailPane(detail);
    }
    return '<div class="status-pill">No detail renderer is available for this item.</div>';
  }

  function renderAttentionInbox() {
    const summaryHost = document.getElementById("attention-inbox-summary");
    const bulkHost = document.getElementById("attention-bulk-bar");
    const gridHost = document.getElementById("attention-inbox-grid");
    if (!summaryHost || !bulkHost || !gridHost) return;

    const items = filteredAttentionItems();
    const selected = selectedAttentionItems();
    const bulkOptions = attentionBulkActionOptions(selected);
    if (state.attention.bulkAction && !bulkOptions.some((option) => option.value === state.attention.bulkAction)) {
      state.attention.bulkAction = "";
    }
    if (!state.attention.detailItemID && items[0] && !state.attention.detailLoading) {
      loadAttentionDetail(items[0].id, { silent: true }).catch(() => {});
    }
    const counts = attentionVisibleStateCounts(items);
    const next = items[0] || state.attention.next;
    const lanes = groupedAttentionLanes(items);

    summaryHost.innerHTML = `
      <div class="attention-summary-strip">
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Visible</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(items.length))} item${items.length === 1 ? "" : "s"} match the current filters.</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Failed</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(counts.failed || 0))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Blocked</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(counts.blocked || 0))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Queued</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(counts.queued || 0))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item attention-summary-next">
          <span class="queue-label">Next Recommended Action</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(next ? attentionDisplayTitle(next) : "Nothing is blocked right now.")}</p>
          <p class="queue-copy attention-command-copy">${escapeHTML(next && next.recommended_command ? next.recommended_command : "No command suggested.")}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">GitHub Feedback</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">Refresh review and reply work items from GitHub notifications.</p>
          <div class="config-actions">
            <button id="attention-feedback-sync-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" ${state.attention.syncingFeedback ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(state.attention.syncingFeedback ? "Syncing..." : "Sync GitHub")}</button>
          </div>
        </article>
      </div>
    `;

    bulkHost.innerHTML = `
      <div class="attention-bulk-shell">
        <div class="attention-bulk-copy">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-attention-select-visible="true" ${items.length ? "" : "disabled"}>Select Visible</button>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-attention-clear="true" ${selected.length ? "" : "disabled"}>Clear</button>
          <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(String(selected.length))} selected</span>
        </div>
        <div class="attention-bulk-controls">
          <label class="selector config-selector">
            <span>Group</span>
            <select id="attention-group-by">
              ${["attention_state", "kind", "repo"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${attentionGroupMode() === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(attentionGroupOptionLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector config-selector">
            <span>Bulk Action</span>
            <select id="attention-bulk-action" ${selected.length ? "" : "disabled"}>
              <option value="">Choose action</option>
              ${bulkOptions.map((option) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.value)}" ${state.attention.bulkAction === option.value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(option.label)} (${escapeHTML(String(option.count))})</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <button id="attention-bulk-apply" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" ${state.attention.bulkAction ? "" : "disabled"}>Apply</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;

    if (!items.length) {
      const emptyMessage = state.attention.loading
        ? "Loading attention inbox..."
        : defaultString(state.attention.error, "No attention items match these filters.");
      gridHost.innerHTML = `
        <div class="attention-board-layout">
          <div class="surface">${buildInlineNotice(emptyMessage)}</div>
          <aside class="surface detail-surface attention-detail-surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h3>Detail</h3>
                <p>Select a tile to inspect it inline.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div id="attention-detail-pane">${renderAttentionDetailPane()}</div>
          </aside>
        </div>
      `;
      return;
    }

    gridHost.innerHTML = `
      <div class="attention-board-layout">
        <div class="attention-board-grid">
          ${lanes.map((lane) => `
            <section class="surface attention-lane" data-attention-lane-shell="${escapeHTML(lane.key)}">
              <div class="surface-head">
                <div>
                  <h3>${escapeHTML(lane.label)}</h3>
                  <p>${escapeHTML(`${lane.items.length} visible item${lane.items.length === 1 ? "" : "s"}`)}</p>
                </div>
                <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(String(lane.items.length))}</span>
              </div>
              <div class="attention-lane-stack">
                ${lane.items.length
                  ? lane.items.map((laneItem) => renderAttentionTile(laneItem, lane.key)).join("")
                  : '<div class="status-pill">No items in this lane.</div>'}
              </div>
            </section>
          `).join("")}
        </div>
        <aside class="surface detail-surface attention-detail-surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Detail</h3>
              <p>Inspect and act on the selected inbox tile without leaving Attention.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="attention-detail-pane">${renderAttentionDetailPane()}</div>
        </aside>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function attentionActionConfirmation(action, count) {
    switch (action) {
      case "approve_work_item":
      case "submit_work_item":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Approve drafts?" : "Approve draft?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Submit ${count} drafted work items to their external targets.`
            : "Submit this drafted work item to its external target.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Approve Drafts" : "Approve Draft",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "approve_planned_item":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Launch planned work?" : "Launch planned work?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Launch ${count} planned work items immediately.`
            : "Launch this planned work item immediately.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Launch Items" : "Launch Item",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "retry_scout_job":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Retry scout jobs?" : "Retry scout job?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Requeue ${count} failed scout jobs for execution.`
            : "Requeue this failed scout job for execution.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Retry Jobs" : "Retry Job",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "resolve_run":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Resolve blocked runs?" : "Resolve blocked run?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Resolve ${count} blocked local runs.`
            : "Resolve this blocked local run.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Resolve Runs" : "Resolve Run",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "launch_issue_work":
        return {
          title: "Start work from issue?",
          message: "Launch implementation for the selected tracked issue.",
          confirmLabel: "Start Work",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "promote_finding":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Promote findings?" : "Promote finding?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Promote ${count} findings into planned work.`
            : "Promote this finding into planned work.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Promote Findings" : "Promote Finding",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "dismiss_finding":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Dismiss findings?" : "Dismiss finding?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Dismiss ${count} findings from the inbox.`
            : "Dismiss this finding from the inbox.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Dismiss Findings" : "Dismiss Finding",
          tone: "danger",
        };
      case "promote_import_candidate":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Promote import candidates?" : "Promote import candidate?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Promote ${count} imported candidates into the findings inbox.`
            : "Promote this imported candidate into the findings inbox.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Promote Candidates" : "Promote Candidate",
          tone: "primary",
        };
      case "drop_import_candidate":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Drop import candidates?" : "Drop import candidate?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Drop ${count} imported candidates.`
            : "Drop this imported candidate.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Drop Candidates" : "Drop Candidate",
          tone: "danger",
        };
      case "drop_approval":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Drop approval items?" : "Drop approval item?",
          message: count > 1
            ? `Remove ${count} approval items from the active queue.`
            : "Remove this approval item from the active queue.",
          confirmLabel: count > 1 ? "Drop Items" : "Drop Item",
          tone: "danger",
        };
      case "drop_run":
      case "drop_work_item":
        return {
          title: count > 1 ? "Drop selected items?" : "Drop selected item?",
          message: count > 1 ? `Remove ${count} selected items from the active queue.` : "Remove this item from the active queue.",
          confirmLabel: "Drop",
          tone: "danger",
        };
      default:
        return null;
    }
  }

  function taskLaunchKindLabel(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "investigation":
        return "Investigation";
      case "manual_scout":
        return "Manual Scout";
      case "local_work":
        return "Coding";
      default:
        return defaultString(value, "Task");
    }
  }

  function taskScheduledItems(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.planned_items || {})
      .filter((item) => ["local_work", "investigation", "manual_scout"].includes(String(item.launch_kind || "").trim()))
      .sort((left, right) => timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at));
  }

  function taskScheduledRows(repo) {
    return taskScheduledItems(repo).map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      title: defaultString(item.title, "(untitled)"),
      launch_kind: taskLaunchKindLabel(item.launch_kind),
      schedule_at: item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "Ready now",
      state: defaultString(item.state, "queued"),
      updated_at: formatDateTime(item.updated_at),
      result: defaultString(item.launch_result || item.last_error, "-"),
      can_launch: item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed",
      can_remove: item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed",
    }));
  }

  function findingStatusLabel(status) {
    switch (String(status || "").trim()) {
      case "promoted":
        return "Promoted";
      case "dismissed":
        return "Dismissed";
      case "resolved":
        return "Resolved";
      default:
        return "Open";
    }
  }

  function findingSourceLabel(finding) {
    switch (String(finding && finding.source_kind || "").trim()) {
      case "manual_scout":
        return `Manual Scout · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      case "investigation":
        return `Investigation · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      case "coding":
        return `Coding Run · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      case "manual_import":
        return `Markdown Import · ${defaultString(finding.source_id, "-")}`;
      default:
        return defaultString(finding && finding.source_kind, "-");
    }
  }

  function findingParentTaskLabel(finding) {
    const kind = defaultString(finding && finding.parent_task_kind, "");
    const id = defaultString(finding && finding.parent_task_id, "");
    return kind && id ? `${kind} · ${id}` : "None";
  }

  function findingPromotedTaskLabel(finding) {
    return defaultString(finding && finding.promoted_task_id, "Not linked");
  }

  function taskFindingRows(items) {
    return (items || []).map((finding) => ({
      id: finding.id,
      title: defaultString(finding.title, "(untitled)"),
      source: findingSourceLabel(finding),
      parent_task: findingParentTaskLabel(finding),
      status: findingStatusLabel(finding.status),
      status_key: defaultString(finding.status, "open"),
      severity: defaultString(finding.severity, "medium"),
      work_type: workTypeLabel(finding.work_type),
      promoted_task: findingPromotedTaskLabel(finding),
      updated_at: formatDateTime(finding.updated_at),
      finding,
    }));
  }

  function renderTaskFindingDetail(repo, finding) {
    const host = document.getElementById("task-finding-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.taskFindings.error && !finding) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.taskFindings.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (state.taskFindings.loading && !finding) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading findings...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!finding) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No finding selected.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const draftScope = taskFindingDraftScope(repo, finding);
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(findingSourceLabel(finding))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.title, "(untitled)"))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.summary, "(no summary)"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Status</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(defaultString(finding.status, "open"), findingStatusLabel(finding.status))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Severity</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.severity, "medium"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(finding.work_type))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Parent Task</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(findingParentTaskLabel(finding))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Promoted Task</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(findingPromotedTaskLabel(finding))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="config-grid" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Title</span>
          <input id="task-finding-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.title, ""))}" />
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Summary</span>
          <textarea id="task-finding-summary" rows="3">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.summary, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Detail</span>
          <textarea id="task-finding-detail-input" rows="6">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.detail, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Evidence</span>
          <textarea id="task-finding-evidence" rows="4">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.evidence, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Severity</span>
          <select id="task-finding-severity">
            ${["low", "medium", "high", "critical"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(finding.severity, "medium") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${value}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Work Type</span>
          <select id="task-finding-work-type">
            ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(finding.work_type, "feature") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
      </div>
      <div class="config-actions">
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-finding-dismiss="${escapeHTML(finding.id)}">Dismiss</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-finding-promote="${escapeHTML(finding.id)}" ${finding.promoted_task_id ? "disabled" : ""}>Promote</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-task-finding-save="${escapeHTML(finding.id)}" ${state.taskFindings.saving ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(state.taskFindings.saving ? "Saving..." : "Save Finding")}</button>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Source Item</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.source_item_id, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Files</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML((finding.files || []).join(", ") || "(none)")}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Path</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(finding.path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Route / Page</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML([defaultString(finding.route, ""), defaultString(finding.page, "")].filter(Boolean).join(" / ") || "(none)")}</p></article>
      </div>
    `;
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
  }

  function findingImportSessionRows(items) {
    return (items || []).map((session) => ({
      id: session.id,
      file_path: defaultString(session.input_file_path, "(inline markdown)"),
      parse_status: defaultString(session.parse_status, "pending"),
      candidate_count: Array.isArray(session.candidates) ? session.candidates.length : 0,
      updated_at: formatDateTime(session.updated_at),
    }));
  }

  function findingImportCandidateRows(session) {
    if (!session || !Array.isArray(session.candidates)) return [];
    return session.candidates.map((candidate) => ({
      candidate_id: candidate.candidate_id,
      title: defaultString(candidate.title, "(untitled)"),
      status: defaultString(candidate.status, "candidate"),
      severity: defaultString(candidate.severity, "medium"),
      work_type: workTypeLabel(candidate.work_type),
    }));
  }

  function renderFindingImportDetail(repo, session, candidate) {
    const host = document.getElementById("task-import-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.findingImports.error && !session) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.findingImports.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (state.findingImports.loading && !session) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading import sessions...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!session) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No import session selected.</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!candidate) {
      host.innerHTML = `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Session</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(session.id)}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">File</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(session.input_file_path, "(inline markdown)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Parse Status</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(session.parse_status, "pending"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        ${session.parse_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(session.parse_error)}</div>` : '<div class="status-pill">Select a candidate to review.</div>'}
      `;
      return;
    }
    const draftScope = findingImportCandidateDraftScope(repo, session, candidate);
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(session.id)}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.title, "(untitled)"))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.summary, "(no summary)"))}</p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="config-grid" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Title</span>
          <input id="task-import-candidate-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.title, ""))}" />
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Summary</span>
          <textarea id="task-import-candidate-summary" rows="3">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.summary, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Detail</span>
          <textarea id="task-import-candidate-detail" rows="6">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.detail, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector config-field-wide">
          <span>Evidence</span>
          <textarea id="task-import-candidate-evidence" rows="4">${escapeHTML(defaultString(candidate.evidence, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Severity</span>
          <select id="task-import-candidate-severity">
            ${["low", "medium", "high", "critical"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(candidate.severity, "medium") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${value}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Work Type</span>
          <select id="task-import-candidate-work-type">
            ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(candidate.work_type, "feature") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
          </select>
        </label>
      </div>
      <div class="config-actions">
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-import-candidate-drop="${escapeHTML(candidate.candidate_id)}" ${candidate.status === "candidate" ? "" : "disabled"}>Drop</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-task-import-candidate-promote="${escapeHTML(candidate.candidate_id)}" ${candidate.status === "candidate" ? "" : "disabled"}>Promote to Finding</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-task-import-candidate-save="${escapeHTML(candidate.candidate_id)}">Save Candidate</button>
      </div>
      ${session.parse_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(session.parse_error)}</div>` : ""}
    `;
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
  }

  function renderTaskInvestigationDetail(detail) {
    const host = document.getElementById("investigation-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.investigations.error && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.investigations.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (state.investigations.detailLoading && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading investigation detail...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!detail || !detail.summary) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">No investigation selected.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const summary = detail.summary;
    const report = detail.final_report;
    const validator = detail.latest_validator_result;
    const investigationPauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason);
    const issueSections = report && Array.isArray(report.issues) && report.issues.length
      ? report.issues.map((issue) => `
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.id, "Issue"))}</span>
          <p class="queue-copy"><strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.short_explanation, "(none)"))}</strong></p>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(issue.detailed_explanation, "(none)"))}</p>
          ${Array.isArray(issue.proofs) && issue.proofs.length ? `
            <ul class="status-list">${issue.proofs.map((proof) => `
              <li>
                <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.title, proof.kind))}</strong>
                <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.why_it_proves, "(no explanation)"))}</span>
                <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.path, defaultString(proof.link, "(no link)")))}</span>
              </li>
            `).join("")}</ul>
          ` : '<div class="status-pill">No proofs attached.</div>'}
        </article>
      `).join("")
      : '<div class="status-pill">No issue-level findings were recorded.</div>';
    const proofSections = report && Array.isArray(report.overall_proofs) && report.overall_proofs.length
      ? `<ul class="status-list">${report.overall_proofs.map((proof) => `
          <li>
            <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.title, proof.kind))}</strong>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.why_it_proves, "(no explanation)"))}</span>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(proof.path, defaultString(proof.link, "(no link)")))}</span>
          </li>
        `).join("")}</ul>`
      : '<div class="status-pill">No overall proofs are available.</div>';
    const validatorContent = validator
      ? `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Accepted</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(String(Boolean(validator.accepted)))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(validator.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        ${Array.isArray(validator.violations) && validator.violations.length ? `
          <ul class="status-list">${validator.violations.map((violation) => `
            <li>
              <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.code, "violation"))}</strong>
              <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.path, "$"))}</span>
              <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(violation.message, "(none)"))}</span>
            </li>
          `).join("")}</ul>
        ` : '<div class="status-pill">No validator violations.</div>'}
      `
      : '<div class="status-pill">No validator result available.</div>';
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.repo_slug, "Workspace"))}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.overall_status, summary.status))}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.query, "(no query)"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Run</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Accepted Round</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.accepted_round, "-"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Issues</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.issue_count, 0))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.updated_at))}</span></div>
          ${investigationPauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(investigationPauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.overall_short_explanation, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Workspace</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.workspace_root, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Final Report</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.final_report_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Last Error</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.last_error, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        ${summary.pause_until ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Until</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.pause_until))}</p></article>` : ""}
        ${summary.pause_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(summary.pause_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Detailed Explanation</h3><p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.completed_at ? formatDateTime(summary.completed_at) : "", "Run not completed yet."))}</p></div></div>
        <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(report && report.overall_detailed_explanation, "(none)"))}</p>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Proofs</h3><p>Primary and supplementary proof links.</p></div></div>
        ${proofSections}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Findings</h3><p>Issue-level conclusions for this investigation.</p></div></div>
        <div class="queue-summary">${issueSections}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Validator</h3><p>Latest validator result for this run.</p></div></div>
        ${validatorContent}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function issueRows(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.issues || {}).sort((left, right) => {
      const leftPriority = left.manual_priority_updated_at ? left.manual_priority : (left.priority ?? 5);
      const rightPriority = right.manual_priority_updated_at ? right.manual_priority : (right.priority ?? 5);
      if (leftPriority !== rightPriority) return leftPriority - rightPriority;
      return left.source_number - right.source_number;
    }).map((issue) => ({
      source_number: issue.source_number,
      title: issue.title,
      work_type: workTypeLabel(issue.work_type),
      priority: issue.manual_priority_updated_at ? `P${issue.manual_priority}` : `P${issue.priority ?? 5}`,
      status: defaultString(issue.status, "-"),
      triage: defaultString(issue.triage_status, "-"),
      schedule_at: issue.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(issue.schedule_at) : "Not scheduled",
      deferred_reason: defaultString(issue.deferred_reason, "-"),
    }));
  }

  function serviceTaskRows(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.service_tasks || {}).map((task) => ({
      kind: defaultString(task.kind, "-"),
      status: defaultString(task.status, "-"),
      issue_key: defaultString(task.issue_key || task.planned_item_id, "-"),
      attempts: task.attempts || 0,
      updated_at: task.updated_at ? formatDateTime(task.updated_at) : "No update yet",
      result: defaultString(task.result_summary || task.last_error, "-"),
    }));
  }

  function plannedItemRows(repo) {
    if (!repo || !repo.state) return [];
    return Object.values(repo.state.planned_items || {}).sort((left, right) => {
      return timestamp(right.updated_at) - timestamp(left.updated_at);
    }).map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
      launch_kind: defaultString(item.launch_kind, "-"),
      priority: `P${item.priority}`,
      schedule_at: item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "Not scheduled",
      state: defaultString(item.state, "-"),
      launch_result: defaultString(item.launch_result || item.last_error, "-"),
    }));
  }

  function repoSchedulerSearchRows(repo) {
    ensureRepoScheduler(repo);
    return (state.repoScheduler.results || []).map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      number: item.number,
      title: item.title,
      labels: Array.isArray(item.labels) && item.labels.length ? item.labels.join(", ") : "-",
      work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
      priority_label: defaultString(item.priority_label, `P${item.priority ?? 3}`),
      updated_at: item.updated_at ? formatDateTime(item.updated_at) : "No update yet",
      target_url: defaultString(item.target_url, ""),
      action_label: item.scheduled ? "Open" : "Add",
      planned_item_id: defaultString(item.planned_item_id, ""),
      scheduled: Boolean(item.scheduled),
      schedule_at: defaultString(item.schedule_at, ""),
    }));
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerSearchResults(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-results");
    if (!host) return;
    host.innerHTML = '<div id="repo-scheduler-search-grid"></div>';
    if (state.repoScheduler.searching) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Searching GitHub issues...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoScheduler.error) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    const rows = repoSchedulerSearchRows(repo);
    renderGrid("repo-scheduler-search-grid", [
      { field: "number", label: "#" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "labels", label: "Labels" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "priority_label", label: "Priority" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      {
        field: "action_label",
        label: "Action",
        render: (row) => row.scheduled
          ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scheduler-open="${escapeHTML(row.planned_item_id)}">Open</button>`
          : `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scheduler-add="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Add</button>`,
      },
    ], rows, {
      maxHeight: "420px",
      emptyMessage: state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery
        ? "No open GitHub issues matched this query."
        : "Search the current repo with GitHub issue qualifiers like label:, assignee:, author:, milestone:, or sort:updated-desc.",
    });
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerSearchPanel(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-panel");
    if (!host) return;
    const draftScope = repoSchedulerSearchDraftScope(repo);
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>Search GitHub Issues</h3>
          <p>Scoped to ${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}. Use GitHub issue qualifiers like label:, assignee:, author:, milestone:, or sort:updated-desc.</p>
        </div>
        <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "manual"))}</span>
      </div>
      <form id="repo-scheduler-search-form" class="scheduler-search-form" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector config-field-wide">
          <span>GitHub Issue Search</span>
          <input id="repo-scheduler-search-query" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.query)}" placeholder="label:bug assignee:octocat sort:updated-desc" />
        </label>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${state.repoScheduler.searching ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.searching ? "Searching..." : "Search")}</button>
      </form>
      ${state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery ? `<p class="queue-copy">Effective query: ${escapeHTML(state.repoScheduler.effectiveQuery)}</p>` : ""}
      <div id="repo-scheduler-search-results"></div>
    `;
    renderRepoSchedulerSearchResults(repo);
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-search-form"));
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerBoard(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-board");
    if (!host) return;
    const items = trackedIssuePlannedItems(repo);
    const widgetKey = "repo-scheduler-board";
    if (!items.length) {
      destroyWidget(state.widgets[widgetKey]);
      delete state.widgets[widgetKey];
      host.innerHTML = buildInlineNotice("No tracked issues are scheduled yet.");
      return;
    }
    const columns = SCHEDULER_BUCKETS.map((bucket) => ({
      id: bucket.id,
      title: bucket.title,
      items: items.filter((item) => schedulerBucketForItem(item) === bucket.id).map((item) => ({
        id: item.id,
        title: item.title,
        description: schedulerCardDescription(item),
        labels: schedulerCardLabels(item),
        priority: schedulerPriorityTone(item.priority),
      })),
    }));
    replaceWidget(widgetKey, Teryx.kanban("#repo-scheduler-board", {
      columns,
      draggable: true,
      onMove(cardId, _fromCol, toCol) {
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(cardId)}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            schedule_at: schedulerScheduleAtForBucket(toCol),
            clear_schedule: toCol === "ready-now",
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = payload.planned_item.id;
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Schedule updated", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Schedule update failed", error.message);
          renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
        });
      },
      onCardClick(card) {
        if (defaultString(selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()) && selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()).id, "") !== defaultString(card && card.id, "")) {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary())));
        }
        state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = card.id;
        renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
      },
    }));
  }

  function renderRepoSchedulerDetail(repo) {
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail");
    if (!host) return;
    const item = selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(repo);
    if (!item) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Select or add a scheduled tracked issue.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const issueNumber = schedulerIssueNumber(item.target_url);
    const draftScope = repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(repo, item);
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo && repo.repo_slug, "Repo"))}${issueNumber ? ` #${escapeHTML(issueNumber)}` : ""}</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(item.title)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_url, "No GitHub issue URL recorded."))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">State</span><span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePill(item.state === "failed" ? "failed" : "queued", item.state)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Work Type</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(item.work_type))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Priority</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(`P${Number(item.priority ?? 5)}`)}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Schedule</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.schedule_at ? formatDateTime(item.schedule_at) : "", "Ready now"))}</span></div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Updated</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at))}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      ${item.last_error ? `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(item.last_error)}</div>` : ""}
      <div class="scheduler-detail-form" data-draft-scope="${escapeHTML(draftScope)}">
        <label class="selector">
          <span>Title</span>
          <input id="repo-scheduler-detail-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(item.title)}" />
        </label>
        <div class="config-grid">
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Priority</span>
            <select id="repo-scheduler-detail-priority">
              ${[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => `<option value="${priority}" ${Number(item.priority ?? 5) === priority ? "selected" : ""}>P${priority}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Work Type</span>
            <select id="repo-scheduler-detail-work-type">
              ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${value}" ${defaultString(item.work_type, "feature") === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
            </select>
          </label>
          <label class="selector">
            <span>Exact Schedule</span>
            <input id="repo-scheduler-detail-schedule" type="datetime-local" value="${escapeHTML(toDateTimeLocal(item.schedule_at))}" />
          </label>
        </div>
        <label class="selector">
          <span>Description</span>
          <textarea id="repo-scheduler-detail-description" rows="5">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.description, ""))}</textarea>
        </label>
        <div class="scheduler-detail-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-scheduler-save="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Save</button>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-scheduler-launch="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Launch Now</button>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-scheduler-delete="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Remove</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, host);
  }

  function renderRepoOverviewPage(repo) {
    const repoRuns = pendingRunsForRepo(repo.repo_slug);
    const repoIssues = issueRows(repo);
    const repoServiceTasks = serviceTaskRows(repo);
    const repoPlannedItems = plannedItemRows(repo);
    const repoWorkItems = pendingWorkItemsForRepo(repo.repo_slug);
    const workSections = [
      renderSurfacePair([
        repoRuns.length ? renderSurface("Pending Jobs", "Work runs mapped to this repo.", '<div id="repo-pending-grid"></div>') : "",
        repoIssues.length ? renderSurface("Issues", "Tracked issues for this repo.", '<div id="repo-issues-grid"></div>') : "",
      ]),
      renderSurfacePair([
        repoServiceTasks.length ? renderSurface("Service Tasks", "Automation work queued or in flight.", '<div id="repo-service-grid"></div>') : "",
        repoPlannedItems.length ? renderSurface("Planned Queue", "Manual launches and scheduled work for this repo.", '<div id="repo-planned-grid"></div>') : "",
      ]),
      repoWorkItems.length ? renderSurface("Work Items", "Inbound items linked to this repo.", '<div id="repo-work-item-grid"></div>') : "",
    ].filter(Boolean).join("");
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:overview`, `
      <section id="repo-metrics" class="metrics-grid metrics-grid-wide"></section>
      <section class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Queue Snapshot</h3>
            <p>Current issue, service, scout-job, and planned-work pressure.</p>
          </div>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-repo-drop="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}">Drop Repo</button>
        </div>
        <div id="repo-queue-summary" class="queue-summary"></div>
      </section>
      ${workSections || `<section class="surface">${buildInlineNotice("No tracked work for this repo.")}</section>`}
    `);

    document.getElementById("repo-metrics").innerHTML = buildMetricCards([
      { label: "Queued Issues", value: repo.issue_counts.queued || 0, note: "Issues waiting to be picked up." },
      { label: "Blocked Issues", value: repo.issue_counts.blocked || 0, note: "Issues blocked on policy, timing, or feedback." },
      { label: "Service Queue", value: (repo.service_task_counts.queued || 0) + (repo.service_task_counts.running || 0), note: "Service tasks still executing or waiting." },
      { label: "Scout Queue", value: repoScoutQueueCount(repo), note: "Local scout jobs waiting, paused, active, or failed." },
      { label: "Dismissed Scouts", value: repoDismissedScoutCount(repo), note: "Saved scout proposals available to retry from the Scouts tab." },
      { label: "Planned Queue", value: repoManualPlannedQueueCount(repo), note: "Manual planned launches that still need action." },
      { label: "Pending Jobs", value: repoRuns.length, note: "Work runs currently mapped to this repo." },
      { label: "Work Items", value: repoWorkItems.length, note: "Inbound items linked to this repo." },
    ]);
    document.getElementById("repo-queue-summary").innerHTML = buildQueueSummary([
      { label: "Repo Mode", value: defaultString(repo.repo_mode, "unknown"), note: "Current repo routing mode." },
      { label: "Issue Pick", value: defaultString(repo.issue_pick_mode, "unknown"), note: "Automation issue pick policy." },
      { label: "PR Forward", value: defaultString(repo.pr_forward_mode, "unknown"), note: "How review and publish are forwarded." },
      { label: "Updated", value: formatDateTime(repo.updated_at), note: "Latest repo state refresh." },
      { label: "Checkout", value: repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Ready" : "Missing", note: repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Managed source checkout is available." : "Managed source checkout has not been hydrated yet." },
      { label: "Source Path", value: defaultString(repo.source_path, "Unavailable"), note: "Mapped path for the managed source checkout." },
      { label: "Last Run", value: repo.last_run ? defaultString(repo.last_run.run_id, "Unknown") : "No run recorded", note: repo.last_run ? formatDateTime(repo.last_run.updated_at || repo.last_run.started_at) : "No completed run metadata." },
    ]);
    if (repoDismissedScoutCount(repo) > 0) {
      document.getElementById("repo-queue-summary").insertAdjacentHTML("beforeend", `
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Dismissed Scout Actions</span>
          <strong class="queue-value">${escapeHTML(String(repoDismissedScoutCount(repo)))}</strong>
          <p class="queue-copy">Open Scouts to retry dismissed proposals and return them to the live queue.</p>
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-open-repo="${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}" data-open-repo-tab="scouts">Open Scouts</button>
        </article>
      `);
    }
    if (repoRuns.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-pending-grid", pendingRunColumns(false), runGridRows(repoRuns, false), {
        maxHeight: "360px",
        emptyMessage: "No pending jobs are mapped to this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoIssues.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-issues-grid", [
        { field: "source_number", label: "#" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "priority", label: "Priority" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status" },
        { field: "triage", label: "Triage" },
        { field: "schedule_at", label: "Scheduled" },
      ], repoIssues, {
        maxHeight: "420px",
        emptyMessage: "No issues are tracked for this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoServiceTasks.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-service-grid", [
        { field: "kind", label: "Kind" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status" },
        { field: "issue_key", label: "Target" },
        { field: "attempts", label: "Attempts" },
        { field: "result", label: "Result" },
      ], repoServiceTasks, {
        maxHeight: "420px",
        emptyMessage: "No service tasks are recorded for this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoPlannedItems.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-planned-grid", [
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "launch_kind", label: "Launch" },
        { field: "priority", label: "Priority" },
        { field: "schedule_at", label: "Schedule" },
        { field: "state", label: "State" },
        { field: "launch_result", label: "Result" },
      ], repoPlannedItems, {
        maxHeight: "420px",
        emptyMessage: "No planned items are queued for this repo.",
      });
    }
    if (repoWorkItems.length) {
      renderGrid("repo-work-item-grid", [
        { field: "source", label: "Source" },
        { field: "subject", label: "Subject" },
        { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.attention_state, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
        { field: "draft_kind", label: "Kind" },
        { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
        { field: "id", label: "Open", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-work-item-show="{{id}}">Open</button>' },
      ], workItemRows(repoWorkItems, false), {
        maxHeight: "360px",
        emptyMessage: "No work items are linked to this repo.",
      });
    }
  }

  function populateIssueSelector(issues) {
    const select = document.getElementById("issue-select");
    if (!select) return;
    if (!issues.length) {
      state.selectedIssue = "";
      select.innerHTML = '<option value="">No tracked issues</option>';
      return;
    }
    if (!state.selectedIssue || !issues.some((issue) => String(issue.source_number) === state.selectedIssue)) {
      state.selectedIssue = String(issues[0].source_number);
    }
    select.innerHTML = issues.map((issue) => {
      const selected = String(issue.source_number) === state.selectedIssue ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${issue.source_number}" ${selected}>#${issue.source_number} ${escapeHTML(issue.title)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  function populatePlannedSelector(items) {
    const select = document.getElementById("planned-select");
    if (!select) return;
    const launchable = items.filter((item) => item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed");
    if (!launchable.length) {
      select.innerHTML = '<option value="">No launchable items</option>';
      return;
    }
    select.innerHTML = launchable.map((item) => {
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">${escapeHTML(item.title)} · ${escapeHTML(item.priority)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
  }

  function renderIssueForm(issue) {
    const host = document.getElementById("issue-form");
    if (!host) return;
    destroyForm("issueForm");
    host.innerHTML = "";
    if (!issue) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Select a tracked issue to edit.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const draftScope = repoControlsIssueDraftScope();
    state.issueForm = Teryx.form("#issue-form", {
      id: "repo-controls-issue-form",
      action: "#",
      method: "post",
      layout: "vertical",
      submitLabel: "Save Issue",
      fields: [
        {
          name: "priority",
          label: "Priority",
          type: "select",
          required: true,
          value: String(issue.manual_priority_updated_at ? issue.manual_priority : (issue.priority ?? 5)),
          options: [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => ({ label: `P${priority}`, value: String(priority) })),
        },
        {
          name: "schedule_at",
          label: "Schedule At",
          type: "datetime-local",
          value: toDateTimeLocal(issue.schedule_at),
        },
        {
          name: "deferred_reason",
          label: "Deferred Reason",
          type: "textarea",
          rows: 3,
          value: issue.deferred_reason || "",
        },
      ],
      onSubmit(data) {
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${state.selectedRepo}/issues/${state.selectedIssue}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            priority: Number(data.priority),
            schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(data.schedule_at),
            deferred_reason: data.deferred_reason,
            clear_schedule: !data.schedule_at,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(draftScope);
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Issue updated", `Issue #${state.selectedIssue} saved.`);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Issue update failed", error.message);
        });
        return false;
      },
    });
    state.issueForm.el.setAttribute("data-draft-scope", draftScope);
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, state.issueForm.el);
  }

  function renderPlannedForm() {
    const host = document.getElementById("planned-form");
    if (!host) return;
    destroyForm("plannedForm");
    host.innerHTML = "";
    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    if (!repo) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Select a repo first.</div>';
      return;
    }
    const launchDefault = repo.repo_mode === "local" ? "local_work" : "github_issue";
    const draftScope = repoControlsPlannedDraftScope();
    state.plannedForm = Teryx.form("#planned-form", {
      id: "repo-controls-planned-form",
      action: "#",
      method: "post",
      layout: "vertical",
      submitLabel: "Create Planned Item",
      fields: [
        { name: "title", label: "Title", required: true, placeholder: "Schedule a maintenance task" },
        { name: "description", label: "Description", type: "textarea", rows: 4, placeholder: "Describe what Nana should do." },
        {
          name: "work_type",
          label: "Work Type",
          type: "select",
          value: "feature",
          options: ["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => ({ label: workTypeLabel(value), value })),
        },
        {
          name: "priority",
          label: "Priority",
          type: "select",
          value: "3",
          options: [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => ({ label: `P${priority}`, value: String(priority) })),
        },
        { name: "schedule_at", label: "Schedule At", type: "datetime-local" },
        {
          name: "launch_kind",
          label: "Launch Kind",
          type: "select",
          value: launchDefault,
          options: [
            { label: "Local Work", value: "local_work" },
            { label: "GitHub Issue", value: "github_issue" },
          ],
        },
      ],
      onSubmit(data) {
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${state.selectedRepo}/planned-items`, {
          method: "POST",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            title: data.title,
            description: data.description,
            work_type: data.work_type,
            priority: Number(data.priority),
            schedule_at: fromDateTimeLocal(data.schedule_at),
            launch_kind: data.launch_kind,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(draftScope);
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          if (state.plannedForm && typeof state.plannedForm.reset === "function") {
            state.plannedForm.reset();
          }
          toast("success", "Planned item added", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Planned item failed", error.message);
        });
        return false;
      },
    });
    state.plannedForm.el.setAttribute("data-draft-scope", draftScope);
    restoreDraftScope(draftScope, state.plannedForm.el);
  }

  function scoutStatusLabel(status) {
    switch (String(status || "").trim()) {
      case "external":
        return "External";
      case "planned":
        return "Planned";
      case "dismissed":
        return "Dismissed";
      default:
        return defaultString(status, "pending").replace(/_/g, " ");
    }
  }

  function scoutActionLabel(action) {
    switch (action) {
      case "promote":
        return "Promote";
      case "retry":
        return "Retry";
      case "dismiss":
        return "Dismiss";
      case "open-run":
        return "Open Run";
      case "reset":
        return "Reset";
      default:
        return action;
    }
  }

  function scoutRoleLabel(roleKey) {
    return repoScoutMeta(String(roleKey || "").replace("-scout", "")).label;
  }

  function workTypeLabel(value) {
    const normalized = String(value || "").trim();
    if (!normalized) return "(untyped)";
    return normalized.replace(/_/g, " ");
  }

  function scoutDestinationLabel(value) {
    switch (String(value || "").trim()) {
      case "review":
        return "Manual Review";
      case "repo":
        return "Repo Issue";
      case "fork":
        return "Fork Issue";
      default:
        return "Auto Promote";
    }
  }

  function scoutItemRows(items) {
    return items.map((item) => ({
      id: item.id,
      title: item.title,
      role: scoutRoleLabel(item.role),
      work_type: workTypeLabel(item.work_type),
      page: defaultString(item.page || item.route, ""),
      severity: defaultString(item.severity, ""),
      audit_mode: defaultString(item.audit_mode, ""),
      destination: scoutDestinationLabel(item.destination),
      status: scoutStatusLabel(item.status),
      status_key: defaultString(item.status === "paused" ? "blocked" : item.status, "pending"),
      pause_reason: defaultString(item.pause_reason, ""),
      pause_until: defaultString(item.pause_until, ""),
      updated_at: formatDateTime(item.updated_at || item.generated_at),
      can_promote: (item.available_actions || []).includes("promote"),
      can_retry: (item.available_actions || []).includes("retry"),
      can_dismiss: (item.available_actions || []).includes("dismiss"),
      can_open_run: (item.available_actions || []).includes("open-run"),
    }));
  }

  function renderScoutDetail(item, hostID = "repo-scout-detail") {
    const host = document.getElementById(hostID);
    if (!host) return;
    if (state.scoutItems.error) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="config-notice">${escapeHTML(state.scoutItems.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }
    if (state.scoutItems.loading && !item) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="status-pill">Loading scout items...</div>';
      return;
    }
    if (!item) {
      host.innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>${escapeHTML(item.title)}</h3>
          <p>${escapeHTML(scoutRoleLabel(item.role))} · ${escapeHTML(scoutDestinationLabel(defaultString(item.destination, "local")))}</p>
        </div>
        ${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(item.status === "paused" ? "blocked" : item.status, "pending"), scoutStatusLabel(item.status), item.pause_until, item.pause_reason)}
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Artifact:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.artifact_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Generated:</strong> ${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.generated_at))}</span>
        <span><strong>Updated:</strong> ${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at || item.generated_at))}</span>
        <span><strong>Area:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.area, "Unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Audit mode:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.audit_mode, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Surface:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.surface_kind, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Target:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.surface_target, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Page:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.page, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Route:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.route, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Work type:</strong> ${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(item.work_type))}</span>
        <span><strong>Severity:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.severity, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Target kind:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_kind, "unknown"))}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Summary</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.summary, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Suggested Next Step</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.suggested_next_step, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Evidence</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.evidence, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Impact</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.impact, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Rationale</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.rationale, "(none)"))}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Files</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.files && item.files.length ? item.files.join(", ") : "(none)")}</p>
        </article>
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Screenshots</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.screenshots && item.screenshots.length ? item.screenshots.join(", ") : "(none)")}</p>
        </article>
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Proposal:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.proposal_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Policy:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.policy_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Preflight:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.preflight_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Issue Drafts:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.issue_draft_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Raw Output:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.raw_output_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Confidence:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.confidence, "unknown"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Labels:</strong> ${escapeHTML(item.labels && item.labels.length ? item.labels.join(", ") : "(none)")}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Browser ready:</strong> ${escapeHTML(String(Boolean(item.browser_ready)))}</span>
        <span><strong>Preflight reason:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.preflight_reason, "(none)"))}</span>
      </div>
      ${(item.recovery_count || item.last_recovery_at || item.last_recovered_run_id) ? `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item">
          <span class="queue-label">Recovery</span>
          <p class="queue-copy">Auto-retry scheduled after stale startup cleanup. Nana keeps the interrupted run in work history and retries this scout proposal once after the cooldown expires.</p>
        </article>
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Recovery Count:</strong> ${escapeHTML(String(Number(item.recovery_count || 0)))}</span>
        <span><strong>Recovered Run:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_recovered_run_id, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Recovery At:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_recovery_at ? formatDateTime(item.last_recovery_at) : "", "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Recovery Reason:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.last_recovery_reason, "(none)"))}</span>
      </div>` : ""}
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Run ID:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.run_id, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Planned Item:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.planned_item_id, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Error:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.error, "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Pause Until:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.pause_until ? formatDateTime(item.pause_until) : "", "(none)"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Pause Reason:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.pause_reason, "(none)"))}</span>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function syncRepoScoutsChrome(selectedCount, allSelected, retryableCount, dismissibleCount) {
    const count = state.scoutItems.items.length || 0;
    const countPill = document.getElementById("repo-scout-count");
    if (countPill) {
      countPill.textContent = `${count} items`;
    }
    const selectAllButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-select-all");
    if (selectAllButton) {
      selectAllButton.disabled = !count;
    }
    const clearButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-clear-selection");
    if (clearButton) {
      clearButton.disabled = !selectedCount;
    }
