    const retryButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-bulk-retry");
    if (retryButton) {
      retryButton.disabled = !retryableCount;
      retryButton.textContent = `Retry Selected (${retryableCount})`;
    }
    const dismissButton = document.getElementById("repo-scout-bulk-dismiss");
    if (dismissButton) {
      dismissButton.disabled = !dismissibleCount;
      dismissButton.textContent = `Dismiss Selected (${dismissibleCount})`;
    }
    const selectionCopy = document.getElementById("repo-scout-selection-copy");
    if (selectionCopy) {
      selectionCopy.textContent = allSelected ? `All ${selectedCount} selected` : `${selectedCount} selected`;
    }
  }

  function renderRepoScoutsPage(repo) {
    ensureScoutItemsState(repo);
    const selectedIDs = selectedScoutItemIDs();
    const selectedSet = new Set(selectedIDs);
    const selectedCount = selectedIDs.length;
    const totalCount = allScoutItemIDs().length;
    const allSelected = totalCount > 0 && selectedCount === totalCount;
    const retryableCount = scoutActionableSelection("retry").length;
    const dismissibleCount = scoutActionableSelection("dismiss").length;
    const gridRows = scoutItemRows(state.scoutItems.items).map((row) => ({
      ...row,
      selected: selectedSet.has(row.id),
    }));
    const gridRenderKey = JSON.stringify({
      loading: Boolean(state.scoutItems.loading),
      error: defaultString(state.scoutItems.error, ""),
      rows: gridRows,
    });
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:scouts`, `
      <section class="surface scout-surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Scout Items</h3>
            <p>Scout findings and proposals saved under the repo checkout.</p>
          </div>
          <span id="repo-scout-count" class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(String(state.scoutItems.items.length || 0))} items</span>
        </div>
        <div class="scout-bulk-bar">
          <button id="repo-scout-select-all" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-select-all="true" ${state.scoutItems.items.length ? "" : "disabled"}>Select All</button>
          <button id="repo-scout-clear-selection" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-clear-selection="true" ${selectedCount ? "" : "disabled"}>Clear</button>
          <button id="repo-scout-bulk-retry" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-bulk-action="retry" ${retryableCount ? "" : "disabled"}>Retry Selected (${escapeHTML(String(retryableCount))})</button>
          <button id="repo-scout-bulk-dismiss" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" data-scout-bulk-action="dismiss" ${dismissibleCount ? "" : "disabled"}>Dismiss Selected (${escapeHTML(String(dismissibleCount))})</button>
          <p id="repo-scout-selection-copy" class="scout-bulk-copy">${escapeHTML(allSelected ? `All ${selectedCount} selected` : `${selectedCount} selected`)}</p>
        </div>
        <div id="repo-scout-grid"></div>
        <div id="repo-scout-detail" class="scout-detail"></div>
      </section>
    `);
    syncRepoScoutsChrome(selectedCount, allSelected, retryableCount, dismissibleCount);
    if (!state.scoutItems.loading && !state.scoutItems.loaded && !state.scoutItems.error) {
      loadScoutItems(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
    renderGrid("repo-scout-grid", [
      {
        field: "id",
        label: "Select",
        render(row) {
          return `<label class="scout-select-cell"><input type="checkbox" class="tx-checkbox" data-scout-toggle="${escapeHTML(row.id)}" ${row.selected ? "checked" : ""} aria-label="Select ${escapeHTML(row.title)}"></label>`;
        },
      },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "role", label: "Role" },
      { field: "page", label: "Page" },
      { field: "severity", label: "Severity" },
      { field: "audit_mode", label: "Audit" },
      { field: "destination", label: "Destination" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePillWithPause(row.status_key, row.status, row.pause_until, row.pause_reason) },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      { field: "id", label: "Details", action: true, template: '<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-select="{{id}}">Details</button>' },
      {
        field: "id",
        label: "Actions",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          const actions = [];
          if (row.can_promote) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="promote" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Promote</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_retry) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="retry" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Retry</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_dismiss) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="dismiss" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Dismiss</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_open_run) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-scout-action="open-run" data-scout-id="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Open Run</button>`);
          }
          return actions.length ? `<div class="scout-actions">${actions.join("")}</div>` : '<span class="data-value-text">No actions</span>';
        },
      },
    ], gridRows, {
      maxHeight: "460px",
      emptyMessage: state.scoutItems.loading ? "Loading scout items..." : "No scout-discovered items found for this repo.",
      preserveScroll: true,
      renderKey: gridRenderKey,
    });
    renderScoutDetail(selectedScoutItem());
  }

  function configStatusPill(enabled) {
    return enabled
      ? '<span class="status-pill">Start Participation: enabled</span>'
      : '<span class="status-pill">Start Participation: disabled</span>';
  }

  function configFieldName(field) {
    const parts = String(field || "").split(".");
    return parts[parts.length - 1] || "";
  }

  function configFieldOptions(field) {
    switch (configFieldName(field)) {
      case "repo_mode":
        return [
          { value: "disabled", label: "Disabled" },
          { value: "local", label: "Local" },
          { value: "fork", label: "Fork" },
          { value: "repo", label: "Repo" },
        ];
      case "issue_pick_mode":
        return [
          { value: "manual", label: "Manual" },
          { value: "label", label: "Label" },
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
        ];
      case "pr_forward_mode":
        return [
          { value: "approve", label: "Approve" },
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
        ];
      case "fork_issues_mode":
      case "implement_mode":
        return [
          { value: "manual", label: "Manual" },
          { value: "labeled", label: "Labeled" },
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
        ];
      case "publish_target":
        return [
          { value: "local-branch", label: "Local Branch" },
          { value: "fork", label: "Fork" },
          { value: "repo", label: "Repo" },
        ];
      case "enabled":
        return [
          { value: "true", label: "Enabled" },
          { value: "false", label: "Disabled" },
        ];
      case "mode":
        return [
          { value: "auto", label: "Auto" },
          { value: "manual", label: "Manual" },
        ];
      case "schedule":
        return [
          { value: "when_resolved", label: "When Resolved" },
          { value: "always", label: "Always" },
          { value: "daily", label: "Daily" },
          { value: "weekly", label: "Weekly" },
        ];
      case "issue_destination":
        return [
          { value: "local", label: "Local" },
          { value: "repo", label: "Repo" },
          { value: "fork", label: "Fork" },
        ];
      default:
        return [];
    }
  }

  function renderConfigSelect(field, label, value, options, disabled = false) {
    const choices = options.map((option) => {
      const selected = String(option.value) === String(value) ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(option.value)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(option.label)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    return `
      <label class="selector config-selector">
        <span>${escapeHTML(label)}</span>
        <select data-config-field="${escapeHTML(field)}" ${disabled ? "disabled" : ""}>${choices}</select>
      </label>
    `;
  }

  function renderConfigInput(field, label, value, options = {}) {
    const type = options.type || "text";
    const min = options.min !== undefined ? ` min="${escapeHTML(String(options.min))}"` : "";
    const max = options.max !== undefined ? ` max="${escapeHTML(String(options.max))}"` : "";
    const placeholder = options.placeholder ? ` placeholder="${escapeHTML(options.placeholder)}"` : "";
    const disabled = options.disabled ? "disabled" : "";
    return `
      <label class="selector config-selector">
        <span>${escapeHTML(label)}</span>
        <input type="${escapeHTML(type)}" value="${escapeHTML(value)}" data-config-field="${escapeHTML(field)}" ${min}${max}${placeholder} ${disabled} />
      </label>
    `;
  }

  function parseConfigFieldValue(field, value) {
    switch (configFieldName(field)) {
      case "enabled":
        return String(value || "") === "true";
      case "labels":
        return String(value || "")
          .split(",")
          .map((label) => label.trim().toLowerCase())
          .filter(Boolean);
      default:
        return value;
    }
  }

  function configScoutPolicyPath(repo, roleKey) {
    const scouts = repoScoutConfigsByRole(repo);
    const config = scouts && scouts[roleKey];
    return defaultString(config && config.policy_path, "");
  }

  function repoNeedsScoutCheckoutBootstrap(repo, draft, server) {
    if (!repo || repo.source_checkout_ready || !draft || !server) return false;
    return repoScoutCatalog(repo).some((entry) => {
      const key = entry.config_key;
      return repoConfigSnapshotKey((draft.scouts_by_role && draft.scouts_by_role[key]) || {})
        !== repoConfigSnapshotKey((server.scouts_by_role && server.scouts_by_role[key]) || {});
    });
  }

  function syncCompatibilityScouts(target) {
    if (!target) return;
    const byRole = target.scouts_by_role || {};
    target.scouts = {
      improvement: byRole.improvement || repoScoutSnapshot("improvement", {}),
      enhancement: byRole.enhancement || repoScoutSnapshot("enhancement", {}),
      ui: byRole.ui || repoScoutSnapshot("ui", {}),
    };
  }

  function setNestedConfigValue(target, field, value) {
    const parts = String(field || "").split(".");
    let cursor = target;
    for (let index = 0; index < parts.length - 1; index += 1) {
      const key = parts[index];
      cursor[key] = { ...(cursor[key] || {}) };
      cursor = cursor[key];
    }
    cursor[parts[parts.length - 1]] = value;
  }

  function renderScoutConfigSection(repo, roleKey, scout) {
    const roleLabel = scoutRoleLabel(roleKey);
    const policyPath = scout.policy_path || configScoutPolicyPath(repo, roleKey);
    const forkDisabled = !scout.enabled || scout.issue_destination !== "fork";
    const sessionLimitField = repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).defaultSessionLimit > 0
      ? renderConfigInput(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.session_limit`, "Session Limit", String(scout.session_limit || repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).defaultSessionLimit), { type: "number", min: 1, max: 6 })
      : "";
    return `
      <div class="config-section">
        <h4>${escapeHTML(roleLabel)}</h4>
        <div class="config-meta">
          <span><strong>Status:</strong> ${escapeHTML(scout.enabled ? "Enabled" : "Disabled")}</span>
          <span><strong>Policy Path:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(policyPath, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="config-grid">
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.enabled`, "Enabled", String(Boolean(scout.enabled)), configFieldOptions("enabled"))}
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.mode`, "Mode", scout.mode, configFieldOptions("mode"))}
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.schedule`, "Schedule", scout.schedule || defaultString(repoScoutMeta(roleKey, repo).defaultSchedule, "when_resolved"), configFieldOptions("schedule"))}
          ${renderConfigSelect(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.issue_destination`, "Destination", scout.issue_destination, configFieldOptions("issue_destination"))}
          ${renderConfigInput(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.fork_repo`, "Fork Repo", scout.fork_repo || "", { placeholder: "owner/repo", disabled: forkDisabled })}
          ${sessionLimitField}
          ${renderConfigInput(`scouts_by_role.${roleKey}.labels`, "Labels", (scout.labels || []).join(", "), { placeholder: "comma,separated,labels" })}
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function updateConfigDraft(field, rawValue) {
    if (!state.configEditor.draft) return;
    const value = parseConfigFieldValue(field, rawValue);
    const next = cloneConfigSnapshot(state.configEditor.draft);
    setNestedConfigValue(next, field, value);
    switch (field) {
      case "repo_mode":
        state.configEditor.overridePublish = false;
        if (value === "disabled") {
          next.publish_target = "";
        } else {
          next.publish_target = repoModeToPublishTarget(value);
        }
        break;
      case "publish_target":
        state.configEditor.overridePublish = true;
        next.repo_mode = publishTargetToRepoMode(value);
        break;
      case "issue_pick_mode": {
        const automationMode = issuePickModeToAutomationMode(value);
        state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = false;
        state.configEditor.overrideImplement = false;
        next.fork_issues_mode = automationMode;
        next.implement_mode = automationMode;
        break;
      }
      case "fork_issues_mode":
        state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = true;
        next.issue_pick_mode = effectiveIssuePickFromAdvanced(next);
        break;
      case "implement_mode":
        state.configEditor.overrideImplement = true;
        next.issue_pick_mode = effectiveIssuePickFromAdvanced(next);
        break;
      default:
        if (field.startsWith("scouts_by_role.")) {
          const parts = field.split(".");
          const roleKey = parts[1];
          const scout = (next.scouts_by_role && next.scouts_by_role[roleKey]) || null;
          if (scout) {
            scout.policy_path = configScoutPolicyPath(selectedRepoSummary(), roleKey);
            if (parts[2] === "issue_destination" && value !== "fork") {
              scout.fork_repo = "";
            }
          }
        }
        break;
    }
    syncCompatibilityScouts(next);
    state.configEditor.draft = next;
    state.configEditor.dirty = !configDraftEquals(next, state.configEditor.server);
    if (!state.configEditor.dirty) {
      state.configEditor.remoteChanged = false;
      state.configEditor.overridePublish = false;
      state.configEditor.overrideForkIssues = false;
      state.configEditor.overrideImplement = false;
    }
    renderRepoConfigPage(selectedRepoSummary());
  }

  function resetConfigDraft(repo) {
    resetConfigEditorForRepo(repo);
    renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
  }

  function saveConfigDraft(repo) {
    if (!repo || !state.configEditor.draft || state.configEditor.saving) {
      return;
    }
    state.configEditor.saving = true;
    renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
    api(`/api/v1/repos/${repo.repo_slug}/settings`, {
      method: "PATCH",
      body: JSON.stringify(state.configEditor.draft),
    }).then((payload) => {
      state.configEditor.saving = false;
      mergeRepoSummary(payload.repo);
      toast("success", "Repo config updated", repo.repo_slug);
    }).catch((error) => {
      state.configEditor.saving = false;
      renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
      toast("danger", "Repo config failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function renderRepoConfigPage(repo) {
    ensureConfigEditor(repo);
    const editor = state.configEditor;
    const draft = editor.draft || repoConfigSnapshot(repo);
    const rawSettings = repo && repo.settings ? repo.settings : {};
    const rawScouts = repo && repo.scouts_by_role ? repo.scouts_by_role : {};
    const needsScoutCheckoutBootstrap = repoNeedsScoutCheckoutBootstrap(repo, draft, editor.server);
    const inventory = [
      { label: "Settings Path", value: defaultString(repo && repo.settings_path, "Unavailable") },
      { label: "Source Checkout", value: repo && repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Ready" : "Missing" },
      { label: "Source Path", value: defaultString(repo && repo.source_path, "Unavailable") },
      { label: "Start State Path", value: defaultString(repo && repo.state_path, "Unavailable") },
    ].concat(repoScoutCatalog(repo).map((entry) => ({
      label: `${scoutRoleLabel(entry.config_key)} Policy`,
      value: defaultString(rawScouts[entry.config_key] && rawScouts[entry.config_key].policy_path, "Unavailable"),
    })));
    const resetDisabled = !editor.dirty && !editor.remoteChanged && !editor.saving;
    const saveDisabled = !editor.dirty || editor.saving;
    const statusCopy = editor.saving
      ? needsScoutCheckoutBootstrap
        ? "Preparing managed checkout and saving scout policies..."
        : "Saving changes..."
      : editor.remoteChanged
        ? "Server config changed while you were editing. Reset to load the latest values."
        : editor.dirty
          ? "Unsaved changes."
          : "All changes saved.";
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:config`, `
      <section class="surface">
        <div id="repo-config-root"></div>
      </section>
    `);
    const host = document.getElementById("repo-config-root");
    if (!host) {
      return;
    }
    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="surface-head">
        <div>
          <h3>Repo Configuration</h3>
          <p>Basic controls set the defaults. Advanced controls and scout policies can override them for this repo.</p>
        </div>
        ${configStatusPill(Boolean(repo.start_participation))}
      </div>
      <div class="config-meta">
        <span><strong>Settings path:</strong> ${escapeHTML(defaultString(repo.settings_path, "Unavailable"))}</span>
        <span><strong>Source checkout:</strong> ${escapeHTML(repo.source_checkout_ready ? "Ready" : "Missing")}</span>
        <span><strong>Updated:</strong> ${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(repo.settings && repo.settings.updated_at))}</span>
      </div>
      <form id="repo-config-form" class="config-form">
        <div class="config-section">
          <h4>Basic Routing</h4>
          <div class="config-grid">
            ${renderConfigSelect("repo_mode", "Repo Mode", draft.repo_mode, configFieldOptions("repo_mode"))}
            ${renderConfigSelect("issue_pick_mode", "Issue Pick", draft.issue_pick_mode, configFieldOptions("issue_pick_mode"))}
            ${renderConfigSelect("pr_forward_mode", "PR Forward", draft.pr_forward_mode, configFieldOptions("pr_forward_mode"))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="config-section">
          <h4>Automation Overrides</h4>
          <div class="config-grid">
            ${renderConfigSelect("fork_issues_mode", "Fork Issues", draft.fork_issues_mode, configFieldOptions("fork_issues_mode"))}
            ${renderConfigSelect("implement_mode", "Implement", draft.implement_mode, configFieldOptions("implement_mode"))}
            ${renderConfigSelect("publish_target", "Publish Target", draft.publish_target || "local-branch", configFieldOptions("publish_target"), draft.repo_mode === "disabled")}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="config-section">
          <h4>Scout Policies</h4>
          <p class="queue-copy">Saving keeps one active policy file per scout under managed scout storage. If the managed source checkout is missing, Nana prepares it before writing scout policies.</p>
        </div>
        ${repoScoutCatalog(repo).map((entry) => renderScoutConfigSection(repo, entry.config_key, draft.scouts_by_role[entry.config_key])).join("")}
        <div class="config-footer">
          <p class="config-status-copy">${escapeHTML(statusCopy)}</p>
          <div class="config-actions">
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-config-reset="true" ${resetDisabled ? "disabled" : ""}>Reset</button>
            <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="submit" ${saveDisabled ? "disabled" : ""}>${escapeHTML(editor.saving ? "Saving..." : "Save Changes")}</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </form>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="config-section">
        <h4>Config Inventory</h4>
        <div class="config-meta">
          ${inventory.map((item) => `<span><strong>${escapeHTML(item.label)}:</strong> ${escapeHTML(item.value)}</span>`).join("")}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="config-section">
        <h4>All Repo Configs</h4>
        <p class="queue-copy">Raw repo settings and scout config payloads currently loaded for this repo.</p>
        <div class="config-json-grid">
          <div class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h4>settings.json</h4>
                <p>Full repo settings payload, including defaults, review rules, and hot-path profile.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(prettyJSON(rawSettings))}</pre>
          </div>
          <div class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h4>Scout Configs</h4>
                <p>Effective per-role scout configuration with the loaded policy paths.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(prettyJSON(rawScouts))}</pre>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function renderRepoControlsPage(repo) {
    ensureRepoScheduler(repo);
    state.taskComposer.repoSlug = defaultString(repo && repo.repo_slug, "");
    ensureTaskFindingsState(repo);
    ensureFindingImportsState(repo);
    if (repo && (!state.taskFindings.loaded || state.taskFindings.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug) && !state.taskFindings.loading) {
      loadTaskFindings(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
    if (repo && (!state.findingImports.loaded || state.findingImports.repoSlug !== repo.repo_slug) && !state.findingImports.loading) {
      loadFindingImports(repo.repo_slug, { silent: true });
    }
    const issues = issueRows(repo);
    const planned = plannedItemRows(repo);
    const launchablePlanned = planned.filter((item) => item.state === "queued" || item.state === "failed");
    const supportsSessionLimit = repoScoutMeta(state.taskComposer.scoutRole, repo).supportsSessionLimit;
    const scheduledRows = taskScheduledRows(repo);
    ensureBodyStructure(`repo:${repo.repo_slug}:controls`, `
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div id="repo-scheduler-search-panel"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Tracked Issue Schedule</h3>
              <p>Drag scheduled tracked issues between buckets. Clicking a card opens exact edit controls.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="repo-scheduler-board"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Selected Scheduled Issue</h3>
              <p>Override the exact launch time or remove the issue from the manual schedule.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="repo-scheduler-detail"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface-stack">
          <section class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h3>Manage Existing Tracked Issue</h3>
                <p>Fallback controls for mirrored start-state issues.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <label class="selector inline-selector">
              <span>Issue</span>
              <select id="issue-select" ${issues.length ? "" : "disabled"}></select>
            </label>
            <div id="issue-form"></div>
          </section>
          <section class="surface">
            <div class="surface-head">
              <div>
                <h3>Create Planned Launch</h3>
                <p>Queue repo-local work or create new GitHub issues.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div id="planned-form"></div>
            <div class="launch-controls">
              <div class="section-divider"></div>
              <div class="stack-section-head">
                <h4>Launch Existing</h4>
                <p>Run a queued planned item immediately.</p>
              </div>
              <label class="selector">
                <span>Launch Existing</span>
                <select id="planned-select" ${launchablePlanned.length ? "" : "disabled"}></select>
              </label>
              <button id="launch-planned-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" ${launchablePlanned.length ? "" : "disabled"}>Launch Now</button>
            </div>
          </section>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Schedule Task</h3>
              <p>Queue investigations, coding work, or manual scout runs for ${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}.</p>
            </div>
            <span class="status-pill">${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="config-grid">
            <label class="config-field">
              <span class="config-label">Task Type</span>
              <select id="task-composer-kind">
                <option value="investigation" ${state.taskComposer.kind === "investigation" ? "selected" : ""}>Investigation</option>
                <option value="coding" ${state.taskComposer.kind === "coding" ? "selected" : ""}>Coding</option>
                <option value="manual_scout" ${state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout" ? "selected" : ""}>Manual Scout</option>
              </select>
            </label>
            <label class="config-field">
              <span class="config-label">Schedule</span>
              <input id="task-composer-schedule" type="datetime-local" value="${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.scheduleAt)}" />
            </label>
            <label class="config-field">
              <span class="config-label">Findings Handling</span>
              <select id="task-findings-handling">
                <option value="review" ${state.taskComposer.scoutDestination === "review" ? "selected" : ""}>Manual Review</option>
                <option value="local" ${state.taskComposer.scoutDestination === "local" ? "selected" : ""}>Auto Promote</option>
              </select>
            </label>
            <label class="config-field config-field-wide">
              <span class="config-label">Task Title</span>
              <input id="task-composer-title" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.title)}" placeholder="${state.taskComposer.kind === "coding" ? "Implement approval retry copy cleanup" : state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout" ? "Run a focused UI scout review" : "Label this investigation task"}" />
            </label>
            <label class="config-field config-field-wide">
              <span class="config-label">Description</span>
              <textarea id="task-composer-description" rows="3" placeholder="${state.taskComposer.kind === "coding" ? "Describe the work Nana should execute." : state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout" ? "Optional notes for why this scout run matters." : "Optional context that should stay attached to the scheduled task."}">${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.description)}</textarea>
            </label>
            ${state.taskComposer.kind === "investigation" ? `
              <label class="config-field config-field-wide">
                <span class="config-label">Investigation Query</span>
                <textarea id="task-investigation-query" rows="4" placeholder="Investigate why approval retry timing drifts between the queue and the drawer.">${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.investigationQuery)}</textarea>
              </label>
            ` : ""}
            ${state.taskComposer.kind === "coding" ? `
              <label class="config-field">
                <span class="config-label">Work Type</span>
                <select id="task-coding-work-type">
                  ${["bug_fix", "refactor", "feature", "test_only"].map((value) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(value)}" ${state.taskComposer.codingWorkType === value ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(value))}</option>`).join("")}
                </select>
              </label>
              <label class="config-field">
                <span class="config-label">Priority</span>
                <select id="task-coding-priority">
                  ${[0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((priority) => `<option value="${priority}" ${String(state.taskComposer.codingPriority) === String(priority) ? "selected" : ""}>P${priority}</option>`).join("")}
                </select>
              </label>
            ` : ""}
            ${state.taskComposer.kind === "manual_scout" ? `
              <label class="config-field">
                <span class="config-label">Scout Role</span>
                <select id="task-scout-role">
                  ${repoScoutCatalog(repo).map((entry) => `<option value="${escapeHTML(entry.role)}" ${state.taskComposer.scoutRole === entry.role ? "selected" : ""}>${escapeHTML(entry.display_label)}</option>`).join("")}
                </select>
              </label>
              ${supportsSessionLimit ? `
                <label class="config-field">
                  <span class="config-label">Session Limit</span>
                  <input id="task-scout-session-limit" type="number" min="1" max="6" value="${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.scoutSessionLimit)}" />
                </label>
              ` : ""}
              <label class="config-field config-field-wide">
                <span class="config-label">Focus</span>
                <input id="task-scout-focus" type="text" value="${escapeHTML(state.taskComposer.scoutFocus)}" placeholder="approvals, retry flow, queue wording" />
              </label>
            ` : ""}
          </div>
          <div class="config-actions">
            <button id="task-schedule-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" ${state.taskComposer.creating ? "disabled" : ""}>${state.taskComposer.creating ? "Scheduling..." : "Schedule Task"}</button>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Scheduled Tasks</h3>
              <p>Queued repo-scoped launches for ${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="task-planned-grid"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Findings Inbox</h3>
              <p>Persisted findings for ${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)} with source lineage and promotion controls.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="config-actions">
              <input id="task-findings-import-file" type="file" accept=".md,text/markdown" />
              <button id="task-findings-import-button" class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm" type="button" ${state.findingImports.importing ? "disabled" : ""}>${state.findingImports.importing ? "Importing..." : "Import Findings from Markdown"}</button>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="task-findings-grid"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface detail-surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Finding Detail</h3>
              <p>Edit persisted findings, dismiss them, or promote them into planned work.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="task-finding-detail"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
      <section class="layout-two-col">
        <div class="surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Import Sessions</h3>
              <p>Markdown imports and candidate findings for ${escapeHTML(repo.repo_slug)}.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="task-import-sessions-grid"></div>
          <div id="task-import-candidates-grid"></div>
        </div>
        <div class="surface detail-surface">
          <div class="surface-head">
            <div>
              <h3>Candidate Detail</h3>
              <p>Review, edit, drop, or promote markdown-derived candidates.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div id="task-import-detail"></div>
        </div>
      </section>
    `);
    populateIssueSelector(issues);
    populatePlannedSelector(planned);
    renderIssueForm(selectedIssueRecord());
    renderPlannedForm();
    renderRepoSchedulerSearchPanel(repo);
    renderRepoSchedulerBoard(repo);
    renderRepoSchedulerDetail(repo);
    renderGrid("task-planned-grid", [
      { field: "launch_kind", label: "Type" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "state", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePill(row.state === "failed" ? "blocked" : row.state, row.state) },
      { field: "schedule_at", label: "Scheduled" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
      {
        field: "id",
        label: "Actions",
        action: true,
        render(row) {
          const actions = [];
          if (row.can_launch) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-task-planned-launch="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Launch Now</button>`);
          }
          if (row.can_remove) {
            actions.push(`<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary tx-btn-sm grid-action-button" type="button" data-task-planned-remove="${escapeHTML(row.id)}">Remove</button>`);
          }
          return actions.length ? `<div class="scout-actions">${actions.join("")}</div>` : '<span class="data-value-text">No actions</span>';
        },
      },
    ], scheduledRows, {
      maxHeight: "340px",
      emptyMessage: "No scheduled tasks are queued for this repo.",
    });
    renderGrid("task-findings-grid", [
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "source", label: "Source" },
      { field: "parent_task", label: "Parent Task" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status", render: (row) => renderStatePill(row.status_key, row.status) },
      { field: "severity", label: "Severity" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
      { field: "promoted_task", label: "Planned Task" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
    ], taskFindingRows(state.taskFindings.items), {
      maxHeight: "420px",
      emptyMessage: state.taskFindings.loading ? "Loading findings..." : defaultString(state.taskFindings.error, "No findings are available for this repo."),
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "finding",
          value: row.id,
          selected: selectedTaskFinding() ? selectedTaskFinding().id === row.id : false,
        };
      },
    });
    renderTaskFindingDetail(repo, selectedTaskFinding());
    renderGrid("task-import-sessions-grid", [
      { field: "id", label: "Session" },
      { field: "file_path", label: "Source File" },
      { field: "parse_status", label: "Parse" },
      { field: "candidate_count", label: "Candidates" },
      { field: "updated_at", label: "Updated" },
    ], findingImportSessionRows(state.findingImports.items), {
      maxHeight: "220px",
      emptyMessage: state.findingImports.loading ? "Loading import sessions..." : defaultString(state.findingImports.error, "No import sessions exist for this repo."),
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "import-session",
          value: row.id,
          selected: selectedFindingImportSession() ? selectedFindingImportSession().id === row.id : false,
        };
      },
    });
    renderGrid("task-import-candidates-grid", [
      { field: "candidate_id", label: "Candidate" },
      { field: "title", label: "Title" },
      { field: "status", label: "Status" },
      { field: "severity", label: "Severity" },
      { field: "work_type", label: "Work Type" },
    ], findingImportCandidateRows(selectedFindingImportSession()), {
      maxHeight: "220px",
      emptyMessage: "No candidates are available for the selected import session.",
      rowSelect(row) {
        return {
          kind: "import-candidate",
          value: row.candidate_id,
          selected: selectedFindingImportCandidate() ? selectedFindingImportCandidate().candidate_id === row.candidate_id : false,
        };
      },
    });
    renderFindingImportDetail(repo, selectedFindingImportSession(), selectedFindingImportCandidate());
  }

  function renderBody() {
    if (state.currentView === "home") {
      renderGlobalPage();
      return;
    }
    if (state.currentView === "usage") {
      ensureViewData("usage");
      renderUsagePage();
      return;
    }
    const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
    const body = document.getElementById("page-body");
    if (!repo) {
      if (state.pageSignature !== "repo-empty") {
        destroyWidgets();
        state.pageSignature = "repo-empty";
      }
      resetScoutItemsState(null);
      body.innerHTML = '<section class="surface empty-surface"><div class="status-pill">No repo is selected.</div></section>';
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoTab === "scouts") {
      renderRepoScoutsPage(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoTab === "config") {
      renderRepoConfigPage(repo);
      return;
    }
    if (state.repoTab === "controls") {
      renderRepoControlsPage(repo);
      return;
    }
    renderRepoOverviewPage(repo);
  }

  function refreshCounts(repo, updatedState) {
    repo.issue_counts = {};
    repo.service_task_counts = {};
    repo.scout_job_counts = {};
    repo.planned_item_counts = {};
    Object.values(updatedState.issues || {}).forEach((issue) => {
      const key = issue.status || "";
      repo.issue_counts[key] = (repo.issue_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    Object.values(updatedState.service_tasks || {}).forEach((task) => {
      const key = task.status || "";
      repo.service_task_counts[key] = (repo.service_task_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    Object.values(updatedState.scout_jobs || {}).forEach((job) => {
      const key = job.status || "";
      repo.scout_job_counts[key] = (repo.scout_job_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
    Object.values(updatedState.planned_items || {}).forEach((item) => {
      const key = item.state || "";
      repo.planned_item_counts[key] = (repo.planned_item_counts[key] || 0) + 1;
    });
  }

  function mergeRepoSummary(updatedRepo, options = {}) {
    if (!state.overview || !updatedRepo) return;
    const index = state.overview.repos.findIndex((entry) => entry.repo_slug === updatedRepo.repo_slug);
    if (index === -1) return;
    const existing = state.overview.repos[index];
    state.overview.repos[index] = {
      ...existing,
      ...updatedRepo,
      state: updatedRepo.state || existing.state || null,
    };
    if (state.configEditor.repoSlug === updatedRepo.repo_slug) {
      resetConfigEditorForRepo(state.overview.repos[index]);
    }
    if (options.resetScouts && state.scoutItems.repoSlug === updatedRepo.repo_slug) {
      resetScoutItemsState(state.overview.repos[index]);
    }
    if (options.rerender !== false) {
      renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
    }
  }

  function mergeRepoState(updatedState) {
    if (!state.overview) return;
    const repo = state.overview.repos.find((entry) => entry.repo_slug === updatedState.source_repo);
    if (!repo) return;
    repo.state = updatedState;
    repo.updated_at = updatedState.updated_at;
    refreshCounts(repo, updatedState);
    reconcileRepoScheduler(repo);
    renderAppPreservingDraftFocus();
  }

  function initLogDrawer() {
    if (state.logDrawer) return;
    state.logDrawer = Teryx.drawer({
      title: "Run Detail",
      position: "right",
      size: "720px",
      content: '<div id="log-drawer-content" class="drawer-shell"></div>',
      onClose() {
        state.logSelection = defaultLogSelection();
        renderLogDrawer();
      },
    });
  }

  function renderLogDrawer() {
    const host = document.getElementById("log-drawer-content");
    if (!host) return;

    if (!state.logSelection.runID) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Choose a run to inspect it.</div>';
      return;
    }

    if ((state.logSelection.loading || state.logSelection.detailLoading) && !state.logSelection.meta && !state.logSelection.detail) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Loading run detail...</div>';
      return;
    }

    if (state.logSelection.error) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="log-empty">${escapeHTML(state.logSelection.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }

    const meta = state.logSelection.meta;
    const detail = state.logSelection.detail;
    if (!meta && !detail) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Run detail is unavailable.</div>';
      return;
    }

    const summary = (detail && detail.summary) || (meta && meta.summary) || {};
    const files = (meta && meta.files) || [];
    const options = files.map((file) => {
      const selected = file.path === state.logSelection.filePath ? "selected" : "";
      return `<option value="${escapeHTML(file.path)}" ${selected}>${escapeHTML(file.path)}</option>`;
    }).join("");
    const manifest = detail ? (detail.github_manifest || detail.local_manifest || null) : null;
    const status = detail && detail.github_status ? detail.github_status : null;
    const typedDetail = detail || {};
    const latestCompletionRound = manifest && Array.isArray(manifest.completion_rounds) && manifest.completion_rounds.length
      ? manifest.completion_rounds[manifest.completion_rounds.length - 1]
      : null;
    const phaseSummary = summary.current_round && !summary.pause_until
      ? `${defaultString(summary.current_phase, "Awaiting phase")} · Round ${summary.current_round}`
      : defaultString(summary.current_phase, "Awaiting phase");
    const runPauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason);
    const laneMarkup = status && Array.isArray(status.lanes) && status.lanes.length
      ? `<ul class="status-list">${status.lanes.map((lane) => `
          <li>
            <strong>${escapeHTML(defaultString(lane.alias, lane.role))}</strong>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(lane.status, "(none)"))}</span>
            <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(lane.role, "(none)"))}</span>
          </li>
        `).join("")}</ul>`
      : '<div class="status-pill">No lane status is available.</div>';
    const manifestSummaryMarkup = typedDetail.backend === "github" && manifest
      ? `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Action</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.next_action, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Human Gate</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.human_gate_reason, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Publication Detail</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status && status.publication_detail, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Final Gate</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status && status.final_gate_status, defaultString(manifest && manifest.final_gate_status, "(none)")))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Candidate Audit</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(status && status.candidate_audit_status, defaultString(manifest && manifest.candidate_audit_status, "(none)")))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Latest Completion</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(latestCompletionRound ? `Round ${latestCompletionRound.round}: ${defaultString(latestCompletionRound.status, "(none)")} · ${defaultString(latestCompletionRound.verification_summary, "(none)")}` : "(none)")}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">External URL</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.external_url, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        </div>
        <div class="section-divider"></div>
        <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Lane Status</h3><p>Per-lane runtime state for this GitHub-backed run.</p></div></div>
        ${laneMarkup}
      `
      : `
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Next Action</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(typedDetail.next_action, defaultString(summary.current_phase, "(none)")))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Sandbox</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(manifest && manifest.sandbox_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Repo Checkout</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(manifest && manifest.sandbox_repo_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Iteration</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(manifest && manifest.current_iteration, "(none)"))}</p></article>
          ${manifest && manifest.superseded_by_run_id ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Superseded By</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(manifest.superseded_by_run_id)}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${manifest && manifest.superseded_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Superseded Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(manifest.superseded_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${manifest && manifest.superseded_at ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Superseded At</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(manifest.superseded_at))}</p></article>` : ""}
        </div>
      `;

    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">Run</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(summary.run_id || state.logSelection.runID)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(runRepoDisplay(summary))} · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.backend, "unknown"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Status</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(summary.attention_state, "active"), defaultString(summary.status, "active"), summary.pause_until, summary.pause_reason)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Phase</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(phaseSummary)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Artifact Root</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(meta && meta.artifact_root, defaultString(summary.artifact_path, "Unavailable")))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Updated</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.updated_at))}</span>
          </div>
          ${runPauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(runPauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Run State</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.target_url, "No target URL recorded."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class="queue-summary">
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Backend</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.backend, "unknown"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Work Type</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(workTypeLabel(summary.work_type))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Publication</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(summary.publication_state, typedDetail.backend === "github" && manifest && manifest.publication_state || "(none)"))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Repo</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(runRepoDisplay(summary))}</p></article>
          <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Current Phase</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(phaseSummary)}</p></article>
          ${summary.pause_until ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Until</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(summary.pause_until))}</p></article>` : ""}
          ${summary.pause_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(summary.pause_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
        </div>
        ${manifestSummaryMarkup}
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        <label class="selector">
          <span>File</span>
          <select id="log-file-select" ${files.length ? "" : "disabled"}>${options || '<option value="">No log files</option>'}</select>
        </label>
        ${typedDetail.resolve_allowed ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-resolve="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Resolve Run</button>` : ""}
        ${typedDetail.sync_allowed ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-sync="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Sync Run</button>` : ""}
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-run-drop="${escapeHTML(summary.run_id)}">Drop Run</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-log-refresh="true">Refresh</button>
      </div>
      ${state.logSelection.loadingContent ? '<div class="status-pill">Loading log content...</div>' : ""}
      <pre class="log-content">${escapeHTML(state.logSelection.content || "No log content available.")}</pre>
    `;
  }

  function openLogDrawer(runID) {
    initLogDrawer();
    state.logSelection = defaultLogSelection();
    state.logSelection.runID = runID;
    renderLogDrawer();
    state.logDrawer.open();
    loadRunDetail(runID);
    loadLogMetadata(runID);
  }

  function loadRunDetail(runID) {
    state.logSelection.runID = runID;
    state.logSelection.detailLoading = true;
    state.logSelection.error = "";
    renderLogDrawer();
    return api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.detail = payload;
      state.logSelection.detailLoading = false;
      renderLogDrawer();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.detailLoading = false;
      state.logSelection.error = error.message;
      renderLogDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Run detail failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function loadLogMetadata(runID, options = {}) {
    state.logSelection.runID = runID;
    state.logSelection.loading = true;
    state.logSelection.error = "";
    renderLogDrawer();
    return api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/logs`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.meta = payload;
      state.logSelection.loading = false;
      const requestedPath = options.preserveFile ? state.logSelection.filePath : "";
      const available = (payload.files || []).map((file) => file.path);
      const filePath = available.includes(requestedPath)
        ? requestedPath
        : (payload.default_path || available[0] || "");
      state.logSelection.filePath = filePath;
      renderLogDrawer();
      if (filePath) {
        return loadLogContent(runID, filePath);
      }
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.loading = false;
      state.logSelection.error = error.message;
      renderLogDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Log load failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function loadLogContent(runID, filePath) {
    state.logSelection.filePath = filePath;
    state.logSelection.loadingContent = true;
    renderLogDrawer();
    const query = new URLSearchParams({ path: filePath, tail: "200" });
    return api(`/api/v1/work/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runID)}/logs/content?${query.toString()}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID || state.logSelection.filePath !== filePath) return;
      state.logSelection.loadingContent = false;
      state.logSelection.content = payload.content || "";
      state.logSelection.error = "";
      if (state.logSelection.meta && payload.summary) {
        state.logSelection.meta.summary = payload.summary;
      }
      renderLogDrawer();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.logSelection.runID !== runID) return;
      state.logSelection.loadingContent = false;
      state.logSelection.error = error.message;
      renderLogDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Log content failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function refreshOpenLogDrawerIfNeeded() {
    if (!state.logSelection.runID || !state.logSelection.meta) return;
    const current = currentRunSummary(state.logSelection.runID);
    if (!current) return;
    const previous = state.logSelection.meta.summary || {};
    if (current.updated_at !== previous.updated_at || current.status !== previous.status || current.current_phase !== previous.current_phase) {
      loadRunDetail(state.logSelection.runID);
      loadLogMetadata(state.logSelection.runID, { preserveFile: true });
    }
  }

  function initWorkItemDrawer() {
    if (state.workItemDrawer) return;
    state.workItemDrawer = Teryx.drawer({
      title: "Work Item",
      position: "right",
      size: "720px",
      content: '<div id="work-item-drawer-content" class="drawer-shell"></div>',
      onClose() {
        state.workItemSelection = defaultWorkItemSelection();
        renderWorkItemDrawer();
      },
    });
  }

  function groupInlineCommentsByPath(comments) {
    const grouped = {};
    (comments || []).forEach((comment) => {
      const key = defaultString(comment.path, "(no path)");
      if (!grouped[key]) {
        grouped[key] = [];
      }
      grouped[key].push(comment);
    });
    return grouped;
  }

  function renderReviewDraftDetail(draft) {
    if (!draft) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">No draft is ready yet.</div>';
    }
    const grouped = groupInlineCommentsByPath(draft.inline_comments || []);
    const groupedHTML = Object.keys(grouped).length
      ? Object.entries(grouped).map(([path, comments]) => `
          <article class="queue-item">
            <span class="queue-label">${escapeHTML(path)}</span>
            <ul class="status-list">
              ${comments.map((comment) => `
                <li>
                  <strong>Line ${escapeHTML(defaultString(comment.line, "-"))}</strong>
                  <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(comment.body, "(none)"))}</span>
                </li>
              `).join("")}
            </ul>
          </article>
        `).join("")
      : '<div class="status-pill">No inline comments were generated.</div>';
    return `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Review Event</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.review_event, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Disposition</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.suggested_disposition, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Confidence</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.confidence, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Review Body</h3><p>Top-level review summary and request.</p></div></div>
      <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.body, "(none)"))}</p>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Inline Comments</h3><p>Grouped by file path.</p></div></div>
      <div class="queue-summary">${groupedHTML}</div>
    `;
  }

  function renderReplyDraftDetail(item, draft) {
    if (!draft) {
      return '<div class="status-pill">No draft is ready yet.</div>';
    }
    return `
      <div class="queue-summary">
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Summary</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.summary, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Comment Kind</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.metadata && item.metadata.comment_kind, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Comment Path</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.metadata && item.metadata.comment_path, "(none)"))}</p></article>
        <article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Comment Line</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.metadata && item.metadata.comment_line, "(none)"))}</p></article>
      </div>
      <div class="section-divider"></div>
      <div class="surface-head"><div><h3>Reply Body</h3><p>Response that will be submitted to the target thread.</p></div></div>
      <p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft.body, "(none)"))}</p>
    `;
  }

  function renderWorkItemDrawer() {
    const host = document.getElementById("work-item-drawer-content");
    if (!host) return;

    if (!state.workItemSelection.itemID) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Choose a work item to inspect it.</div>';
      return;
    }

    if (state.workItemSelection.loading && !state.workItemSelection.detail) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Loading work item...</div>';
      return;
    }

    if (state.workItemSelection.error) {
      host.innerHTML = `<div class="log-empty">${escapeHTML(state.workItemSelection.error)}</div>`;
      return;
    }

    const detail = state.workItemSelection.detail;
    if (!detail || !detail.item) {
      host.innerHTML = '<div class="log-empty">Work item details are unavailable.</div>';
      return;
    }

    const item = detail.item;
    const draft = item.latest_draft || null;
    const workItemPauseSummary = pauseStateSummary(item.pause_until, item.pause_reason);
    const showRestoreButton = Boolean(item.hidden || item.status === "dropped");
    const events = (detail.events || []).map((event) => {
      return `
        <li>
          <strong>${escapeHTML(event.event_type)}</strong>
          <span>${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(event.created_at))}</span>
          <span>${escapeHTML(defaultString(event.actor, "-"))}</span>
        </li>
      `;
    }).join("");

    host.innerHTML = `
      <div class="drawer-summary">
        <div>
          <span class="drawer-label">Item</span>
          <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(item.id)}</span>
          <p class="drawer-copy">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source, "-"))}/${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.source_kind, "-"))} · ${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.repo_slug, "Standalone"))}</p>
        </div>
        <div class="drawer-summary-grid">
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Status</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${renderStatePillWithPause(defaultString(currentWorkItemSummary(item.id)?.attention_state, "active"), defaultString(item.status, "-"), item.pause_until, item.pause_reason)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Target</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.target_url, "Unavailable"))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Linked Run</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.linked_run_id, "-"))}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="drawer-summary-card">
            <span class="drawer-label">Updated</span>
            <span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.updated_at))}</span>
          </div>
          ${workItemPauseSummary ? `<div class="drawer-summary-card"><span class="drawer-label">Retry</span><span class="drawer-value">${escapeHTML(workItemPauseSummary)}</span></div>` : ""}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="drawer-toolbar">
        ${item.status === "paused" ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-requeue="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Return to Queue</button>` : ""}
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-run="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Run</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-fix="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Fix</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-primary" type="button" data-work-item-submit="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Submit</button>
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-drop="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Drop</button>
        ${showRestoreButton ? `<button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-restore="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Restore</button>` : ""}
        <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-refresh="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Refresh</button>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.subject, "(no subject)"))}</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(item.body, "No source body captured."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${(item.pause_until || item.pause_reason) ? `
          <div class="queue-summary">
            ${item.pause_until ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Until</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(formatDateTime(item.pause_until))}</p></article>` : ""}
            ${item.pause_reason ? `<article class="queue-item"><span class="queue-label">Pause Reason</span><p class="queue-copy">${escapeHTML(item.pause_reason)}</p></article>` : ""}
          </div>
        ` : ""}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Draft</h3>
            <p>${escapeHTML(defaultString(draft ? draft.summary : "", draft ? "Review the current draft before submission." : "No draft is ready yet."))}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${draft && draft.kind === "review"
          ? renderReviewDraftDetail(draft)
          : renderReplyDraftDetail(item, draft)}
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Revise Draft</h3>
            <p>Write an instruction for Nana to revise the current draft.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <label class="selector config-selector">
          <span>Instruction</span>
          <textarea id="work-item-fix-instruction" rows="4" placeholder="Clarify the justification and tighten the reply.">${escapeHTML(state.workItemSelection.fixInstruction || "")}</textarea>
        </label>
        <div class="config-actions">
          <button class="tx-btn tx-btn-secondary" type="button" data-work-item-fix="${escapeHTML(item.id)}">Apply Revision</button>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="surface">
        <div class="surface-head">
          <div>
            <h3>Events</h3>
            <p>Audit history for this item.</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        ${events ? `<ul class="status-list">${events}</ul>` : '<div class="status-pill">No events are recorded yet.</div>'}
      </div>
    `;
  }

  function openWorkItemDrawer(itemID) {
    initWorkItemDrawer();
    state.workItemSelection = defaultWorkItemSelection();
    state.workItemSelection.itemID = itemID;
    state.workItemSelection.loading = true;
    renderWorkItemDrawer();
    state.workItemDrawer.open();
    loadWorkItemDetail(itemID);
  }

  function loadWorkItemDetail(itemID) {
    state.workItemSelection.itemID = itemID;
    state.workItemSelection.loading = true;
    state.workItemSelection.error = "";
    renderWorkItemDrawer();
    return api(`/api/v1/work-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`).then((payload) => {
      if (state.workItemSelection.itemID !== itemID) return;
      state.workItemSelection.loading = false;
      state.workItemSelection.detail = payload;
      state.workItemSelection.fixInstruction = "";
      renderWorkItemDrawer();
    }).catch((error) => {
      if (state.workItemSelection.itemID !== itemID) return;
      state.workItemSelection.loading = false;
      state.workItemSelection.error = error.message;
      renderWorkItemDrawer();
      toast("danger", "Work item failed", error.message);
    });
  }

  function refreshOpenWorkItemDrawerIfNeeded() {
    if (!state.workItemSelection.itemID || !state.workItemSelection.detail) return;
    const current = currentWorkItemSummary(state.workItemSelection.itemID);
    const previous = state.workItemSelection.detail.item || {};
    if (!current) return;
    if (current.updated_at !== previous.updated_at || current.status !== previous.status) {
      loadWorkItemDetail(state.workItemSelection.itemID);
    }
  }

  function renderApp() {
    if (!state.overview && !canRenderWithoutOverview(state.currentView)) {
      syncUsageAutoRefresh();
      return;
    }
    ensureSelection();
    renderSidebar();
    renderHeader();
    renderBreadcrumbs();
    renderQuickSwitchOptions();
    renderTabs();
    renderBody();
    renderConfirmDialog();
    syncHashState();
    syncUsageAutoRefresh();
    refreshOpenLogDrawerIfNeeded();
    refreshOpenWorkItemDrawerIfNeeded();
  }

  function attachHandlers() {
    document.getElementById("refresh-button").addEventListener("click", () => {
      load();
      if (state.currentView !== "usage") {
        refreshCurrentView({ silent: true });
      }
      if (state.currentView === "repo" && state.repoTab === "scouts" && state.selectedRepo) {
        loadScoutItems(state.selectedRepo, { silent: true });
      }
      if (state.currentView === "repo" && state.repoTab === "controls" && state.selectedRepo) {
        loadTaskFindings(state.selectedRepo, { silent: true });
        loadFindingImports(state.selectedRepo, { silent: true });
      }
      if (state.logSelection.runID) {
        loadRunDetail(state.logSelection.runID);
        loadLogMetadata(state.logSelection.runID, { preserveFile: true });
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("quick-switch-button").addEventListener("click", () => {
      runQuickSwitch();
    });

    document.getElementById("quick-switch-input").addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      if (event.key === "Enter") {
        event.preventDefault();
        runQuickSwitch();
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("sidebar-nav").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      if (event.target.closest("[data-view-filter-reset]")) {
        event.preventDefault();
        event.stopPropagation();
        return;
      }
      const onboardButton = event.target.closest("[data-open-onboard]");
      if (onboardButton) {
        clearDraftsForRouteTransition({ view: "home", repoSlug: state.selectedRepo, repoTab: state.repoTab });
        state.currentView = "home";
        renderApp();
        window.setTimeout(() => {
          const input = document.getElementById("repo-onboard-slug");
          if (input) input.focus();
        }, 0);
        return;
      }
      const button = event.target.closest("[data-nav-view]");
      if (!button) return;
      const nextView = button.getAttribute("data-nav-view");
      if (nextView && nextView !== "repo") {
        clearDraftsForRouteTransition({ view: nextView, repoSlug: state.selectedRepo, repoTab: state.repoTab });
        state.currentView = nextView;
        ensureViewData(nextView);
        renderApp();
        return;
      }
      const repoSlug = button.getAttribute("data-repo-slug");
      if (!repoSlug) return;
      openRepoView(repoSlug, "overview");
    });

    document.getElementById("sidebar-nav").addEventListener("input", (event) => {
      if (!event.target.matches("[data-sidebar-query]")) return;
      const caret = typeof event.target.selectionStart === "number" ? event.target.selectionStart : null;
      state.sidebarQuery = String(event.target.value || "");
      renderSidebar();
      const nextInput = document.querySelector("[data-sidebar-query]");
      if (nextInput) {
        nextInput.focus();
        if (caret !== null && typeof nextInput.setSelectionRange === "function") {
          nextInput.setSelectionRange(caret, caret);
        }
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-tabs").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const button = event.target.closest("[data-tab-group]");
      if (!button) return;
      const group = button.getAttribute("data-tab-group");
      const tabID = button.getAttribute("data-tab-id") || "";
      if (group === "repo") {
        clearDraftsForRouteTransition({ view: "repo", repoSlug: state.selectedRepo, repoTab: tabID || "overview" });
        state.repoTab = tabID || "overview";
        ensureViewData("repo");
        renderApp();
      }
    });

    document.getElementById("page-tabs").addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
      const tab = event.target.closest("[data-tab-group]");
      if (!tab) return;
      if (!["ArrowLeft", "ArrowRight", "Home", "End"].includes(event.key)) return;
      event.preventDefault();
      const group = tab.getAttribute("data-tab-group");
      const tabs = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(`[data-tab-group="${group}"]`));
      const currentIndex = tabs.indexOf(tab);
      if (currentIndex === -1) return;
      let nextIndex = currentIndex;
      if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
        nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % tabs.length;
      } else if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
        nextIndex = (currentIndex - 1 + tabs.length) % tabs.length;
      } else if (event.key === "Home") {
        nextIndex = 0;
      } else if (event.key === "End") {
        nextIndex = tabs.length - 1;
      }
      tabs[nextIndex].focus();
      tabs[nextIndex].click();
    });

    document.getElementById("page-body").addEventListener("click", (event) => {
      const repoButton = event.target.closest("[data-open-repo]");
      if (repoButton) {
        openRepoView(
          repoButton.getAttribute("data-open-repo") || "",
          repoButton.getAttribute("data-open-repo-tab") || "overview",
        );
        return;
      }

      const attentionSelectVisibleButton = event.target.closest("[data-attention-select-visible]");
      if (attentionSelectVisibleButton) {
        selectAllVisibleAttentionItems();
        renderAttentionInbox();
        return;
      }

      const attentionClearButton = event.target.closest("[data-attention-clear]");
      if (attentionClearButton) {
        clearAttentionSelection();
        renderAttentionInbox();
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "attention-feedback-sync-button") {
        syncGithubFeedbackFromAttention().catch(() => {});
        return;
      }

      const attentionOpenButton = event.target.closest("[data-attention-open]");
      if (attentionOpenButton) {
        const item = attentionItemByID(attentionOpenButton.getAttribute("data-attention-open") || "");
        if (item) {
          openAttentionItem(item);
        }
        return;
      }

      const attentionActionButton = event.target.closest("[data-attention-action]");
      if (attentionActionButton) {
        const action = attentionActionButton.getAttribute("data-attention-action") || "";
        const item = attentionItemByID(attentionActionButton.getAttribute("data-attention-item-id") || "");
        if (item && action) {
          executeAttentionAction(action, [item]);
        }
        return;
      }

      const attentionDetailActionButton = event.target.closest("[data-attention-detail-action]");
      if (attentionDetailActionButton) {
        const action = attentionDetailActionButton.getAttribute("data-attention-detail-action") || "";
        const item = attentionItemByID(attentionDetailActionButton.getAttribute("data-attention-detail-item-id") || "") || attentionDetailItem();
        if (item && action) {
          executeAttentionAction(action, [item], { payload: attentionActionPayload(action), ignoreSummary: true });
        }
        return;
      }

      if (event.target.id === "attention-bulk-apply") {
        executeAttentionAction(state.attention.bulkAction, selectedAttentionItems());
        return;
      }

      const attentionTile = event.target.closest("[data-attention-tile]");
      if (attentionTile && !event.target.closest("button, a, input, select, textarea, label")) {
        const item = attentionItemByID(attentionTile.getAttribute("data-attention-tile") || "");
        if (item) {
          openAttentionItem(item);
        }
        return;
      }

      if (!event.target.closest("button, a, input, select, textarea, summary")) {
        const rowSelect = event.target.closest("[data-row-select-kind]");
        if (rowSelect) {
          const kind = rowSelect.getAttribute("data-row-select-kind");
          const value = rowSelect.getAttribute("data-row-select-id") || "";
          if (kind === "finding") {
            if (defaultString(selectedTaskFinding() && selectedTaskFinding().id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(taskFindingDraftScope(selectedTaskRepoSummary(), selectedTaskFinding()));
            }
            state.taskFindings.selectedFindingID = value;
            rerenderRepoControlsSurface();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "import-session") {
            if (defaultString(selectedFindingImportSession() && selectedFindingImportSession().id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(selectedTaskRepoSummary(), selectedFindingImportSession(), selectedFindingImportCandidate()));
            }
            state.findingImports.selectedSessionID = value;
            state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = "";
            const session = selectedFindingImportSession();
            if (session && session.candidates && session.candidates[0]) {
              state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = session.candidates[0].candidate_id;
            }
            rerenderRepoControlsSurface();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "import-candidate") {
            if (defaultString(selectedFindingImportCandidate() && selectedFindingImportCandidate().candidate_id, "") !== value) {
              clearDraftScope(findingImportCandidateDraftScope(selectedTaskRepoSummary(), selectedFindingImportSession(), selectedFindingImportCandidate()));
            }
            state.findingImports.selectedCandidateID = value;
            rerenderRepoControlsSurface();
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "run") {
            openLogDrawer(value);
            return;
          }
          if (kind === "work-item") {
            openWorkItemDrawer(value);
            return;
          }
        }
      }

      const repoDropButton = event.target.closest("[data-repo-drop]");
      if (repoDropButton) {
        const repoSlug = repoDropButton.getAttribute("data-repo-drop");
        if (repoSlug) {
          dropRepo(repoSlug);
        }
        return;
      }

      const schedulerOpenButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-open]");
      if (schedulerOpenButton) {
        const nextPlannedItemID = schedulerOpenButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-open") || "";
        if (defaultString(selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()) && selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()).id, "") !== nextPlannedItemID) {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary())));
        }
        state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = nextPlannedItemID;
        renderRepoControlsPage(selectedRepoSummary());
        return;
      }

      const schedulerAddButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-add]");
      if (schedulerAddButton) {
        const resultID = schedulerAddButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-add") || "";
        const repo = selectedRepoSummary();
        const result = (state.repoScheduler.results || []).find((item) => item.id === resultID);
        if (!repo || !result) return;
        api(`/api/v1/repos/${repo.repo_slug}/tracked-issues/schedule`, {
          method: "POST",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            number: result.number,
            title: result.title,
            target_url: result.target_url,
            labels: result.labels || [],
            work_type: result.work_type || "",
            priority: result.priority,
          }),
        }).then((payload) => {
          clearDraftScope(repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(repo, selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(repo)));
          state.repoScheduler.selectedPlannedItemID = payload.planned_item.id;
          mergeRepoState(payload.state);
          toast("success", "Tracked issue scheduled", payload.planned_item.title);
        }).catch((error) => {
          toast("danger", "Schedule failed", error.message);
        });
        return;
      }

      const schedulerSaveButton = event.target.closest("[data-scheduler-save]");
      if (schedulerSaveButton) {
        const itemID = schedulerSaveButton.getAttribute("data-scheduler-save") || "";
        const draftScope = repoSchedulerDetailDraftScope(selectedRepoSummary(), selectedTrackedIssuePlannedItem(selectedRepoSummary()));
        const titleInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-title");
        const priorityInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-priority");
        const workTypeInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-work-type");
        const scheduleInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-schedule");
        const descriptionInput = document.getElementById("repo-scheduler-detail-description");
        api(`/api/v1/planned-items/${encodeURIComponent(itemID)}`, {
          method: "PATCH",
          body: JSON.stringify({
            title: titleInput ? String(titleInput.value || "").trim() : "",
            description: descriptionInput ? String(descriptionInput.value || "") : "",
